Seeing the Light Again 39

The Divine Skill of an Ophthalmologist

(London) Watson, an Englishman, suffered from measles at the age of two, which caused him to lose his sight. Now at the age of twenty-nine, he thought he would never see the light again. He has now met Dr. Thomas, an ophthalmologist, who believes that he can be cured. He performed a very skillful operation today, taking the corneas from the eyes of two others and transplanting them. As a result, Watson, who had not seen the light of day for twenty-seven years, actually saw the light again. This amazing achievement has attracted considerable attention. Many famous surgeons, such as Elder, have entered the hospital to inspect it. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Investigation Report on the Accident of the Soviet Russian Balloon 40

The Accident Occurred at 4:10 PM on Tuesday

The Balloon Compartment Broke Off and Touched Ground at 4:23 PM

It Had Risen to an Altitude of 22,000 Meters

It Continued to Record Even During the Sudden Descent

(Moscow) The special committee investigating the details of the accident of the Soviet Russian stratosphere balloon "Sirihes" today released a report stating that the three aeronauts continued to record as they ascended into the stratosphere, even during the beginning of the sharp descent to the ground. Although many of the delicate scientific instruments in the balloon were shattered, the tape recording the pressure instruments inside the balloon chamber remained intact, indicating that the balloon reached its maximum height at 12:33 PM on Tuesday. As for the cause of the accident, it was found that the descent began at 12:45 PM, and the descent became faster and faster. By 4:10 PM, at an altitude of 12,000 meters, the rate of descent was alarming. The sudden acceleration caused part of the rope holding the balloon chamber to break, and the aluminum chamber tilted and separated from the balloon. It touched the ground at 4:23 PM and was destroyed with great force. The committee determined that the last recording was at 4:10 PM and now recognizes this as the starting point of the disaster. All previous recordings are sufficient to prove that the three aeronauts were in high spirits and excited about the success of the ascent. (National News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

(Moscow) According to the results of the examination, the reason for the accident of the Soviet Russian stratosphere exploration balloon "Sirius" was caused by the icing outside the balloon chamber and on the ropes. Because the balloon had risen into the atmosphere where the air was violently shaken, the balloon swayed up and down, and the ropes had iced, which caused them to break into small pieces, and the balloon fell. (National News Agency dispatch, 1st)

(Moscow) The "Sirihes" stratosphere balloon recorded that the balloon had risen to a height of 22,000 meters, which is 1,400 meters higher than previously announced and 3,000 meters higher than the height reached by the first Soviet Russian stratosphere balloon. (National News Agency dispatch, 1st)

Anglo-French Trade War Unavoidable 41

Britain Demands that France Restore Import Quantities

Declares that Retaliation Will Be Taken if Refused

(Paris) The trade war between Britain and France seems inevitable unless a negotiated settlement is reached at the last minute. It is reported that the French government has rejected the British demand to restore the old import quotas for British goods, and Britain has declared that if France does not agree to restore the previous import quotas for British goods within ten days, that is, before February 8, it will take retaliatory measures against French goods. Officials have not revealed the details of the French reply, but it is widely believed that its content is that France demands equivalent benefits because France must make up for its commercial losses in order to achieve balance. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

The Future of Arms Reduction Remains Chaotic After Concrete Expressions from Britain and Italy 42

London Eagerly Awaits Responses from Various Countries

Will the Gap Between France and Germany Widen?

The Key to the Future Lies in French Concessions

(London) London is now eagerly awaiting prompt responses from France, Germany, and other countries to the British memorandum, and hopes that their second thoughts can change the informal reactions. Judging from the informal reactions, the gap between France and Germany will widen. British officials acknowledge that France must make major concessions, but it can also obtain valuable rewards, namely, first, Germany's return to the League of Nations, and second, Germany's acceptance of permanent automatic inspections on military preparations.

French newspapers are almost unanimously opposed. The Labor newspaper's headline reads, "Simultaneous Attack from London and Rome." The Paris Echo newspaper does not even approve of the compromise, saying that the compromise gives unfair preferential treatment to those who demand too much.

Italian newspapers believe that the simultaneous publication of the British and Italian memorandums is proof that the two governments agreed on it in advance. A Washington dispatch states that the British memorandum and President Roosevelt's gold announcement are viewed as equally important in official circles.

A semi-official document from Berlin is quite pleased with the British and Italian memorandums' recognition of Germany's demand for equality, and therefore believes that this is a major and valuable contribution to European peace. German newspapers especially welcome the Italian proposal because its memorandum does not mention military aircraft and does not say a word about Germany's return to Geneva. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

French Arms Reduction Note 43

Gentle Wording with No Surprises

Still Difficult for Germany and France to Approach Each Other

(Paris) The French government's memorandum answering Germany's arms reduction construction of a month ago was released today. The content of the document is indeed as expected outside when it was sent to Berlin and has no surprises. Its wording is very gentle, expressing the French government's intention to strive for reconciliation, and its nature is to seek new ways so that the arms reduction conference can be reopened. France does not allow Germany's standing army to exceed 200,000 people (Germany believes that 200,000 people is not enough to guarantee its security). France is willing to reduce 50% of its air force strength, but the demobilized parts are still retained for future international air force use (Germany believes that if Germany is not allowed to equip an air force, then France's proposal is worthless). France is willing to put forward formal suggestions in Geneva (Germany is willing to negotiate directly because it has no intention of returning to the "Capital of Peace"). France has put forward suggestions for a trial period of arms reduction (Germany believes that this is a discriminatory move against Germany). France suggests that international supervision should be imposed on German paramilitary organizations (Germany insists that any supervision imposed on Germany should also be imposed on other countries). The full text of the memorandum is fifteen pages long. Germany has carefully studied it in the middle of last month. The general opinion is that this document cannot bring the positions of Germany and France closer. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

(Paris) On January 1st of this year, French Ambassador to Germany Ponset handed over the French government's arms reduction memorandum to German Chancellor Hitler. Its content was not released until today. The main points are as follows: The memorandum first raises reservations about the reasons on which Germany's demands are based, especially regarding Germany's rearmament.

Non-Aggression Treaty 44

Secondly, it expressed satisfaction with Germany's intention to conclude non-aggression treaties with its neighboring countries, but stated that non-aggression treaties can only be established if they do not harm the scope of security guarantees stipulated in existing treaties. Among the existing treaties, the Locarno Treaty is especially important, and non-aggression treaties must add other new guarantees to it so that the contracting countries can maintain their independence and are not subject to external threats, and their internal affairs are not subject to foreign interference."

Military Inspection System 45

Then it stated that since Germany has already approved

In principle, the system of on-site, on-time, automatic military inspection, it is not known whether it can accept the implementation methods proposed during the last few discussions of the arms reduction conference. Other parties are likely to agree on this level. The memorandum also stated that the arms reduction conference has clearly indicated its goals up to now, and Germany has no objection. Now Germany's proposal to substantially rearm is contrary to this goal. The reason why Germany's plan to substantially rearm cannot be implemented immediately is only limited by the financial situation.

Troop Size and Military Equipment 46

Although the troop size demanded by Germany is 300,000 people,

In addition to this number, there are still a large number of police, whose military nature has been recognized by the arms reduction conference, and there are also military education organizations outside the formal army. No draft convention has calculated these organizations as troop quotas. Therefore, the name is 300,000 people, but it is unknown how many there are in reality. It is too unfair to compare this with other countries. Regarding the issue of military equipment, the memorandum stated that Germany's demand to immediately rearm in terms of quantity and quality is, in fact, if it is to be implemented fairly, it is necessary to first plan the standardization of the military systems of various countries, and the unification of military systems cannot be achieved without several years of effort. Germany also acknowledges this level. As for the military inspection system, although Germany has approved it in principle, it has raised reservations about the implementation period. It is unknown whether the future arms reduction convention can be effectively implemented, and it all depends on whether the inspection system can be accurately used. Moreover, the demands proposed by Germany are no different from a complete plan for rearmament. If this plan is approved by the future arms reduction convention, what is the difference from reopening the door to the arms race?

Phased Disarmament System 47

On the French side, it is prepared to accept another plan, namely, to revise the British arms reduction proposal according to the unstable situation of European politics and the necessary conditions for implementation, so as to achieve phased restrictions on military preparations and fully realize the principle of equality. France intends to reduce the number of French troops in the first few years of the arms reduction convention, referring to the conscription system adopted by the German National Defense Forces, in the hope of making the military organization of the two countries consistent. France also recognizes that all military equipment is limited to the existing level and will not be increased. France is also willing to stop manufacturing any military equipment with a caliber exceeding the limits permitted by the convention. This is called the first phase. Also, within this period, the military inspection system must be adjusted, and it applies to the number of troops and the manufacture and import of military equipment in various countries. After this, all military equipment that exceeds the limit in quality will be gradually abolished, and countries that are currently restricted by peace treaties will also gradually be allowed to equip them. France is willing to specify the numbers for the above points and include them in the arms reduction convention. However, in order to seek practical results when discussing this issue, the countries concerned should consult together. This is called the second phase.

Air Force Reduced by 50% 48

In order for France to show the importance of the second phase of disarmament to Germany, it has specially cited several examples in the memorandum to cover the rest. For example, the caliber of active guns can be reduced by France to 155 meters, which is the caliber allowed by the future convention. In addition, France plans to reduce 50% of its existing air force equipment within a few years of the start of the arms reduction convention, provided that the air forces of major countries are reduced as many as possible, and effective supervision is implemented on the establishment and manufacture of civil aviation.

International Air Force System 49

The memorandum also stated that the military aviation of all countries should be abolished in full and replaced by an international air force. France is preparing to reduce military preparations on a large scale, so it can be seen that this is the opposite of what Germany said. However, it still relies on Germany's cooperation. The memorandum also explained that France has no intention of closing the door to current negotiations. The French government is pleased that the German government has stated that Chancellor Hitler is prepared to resolve any future disputes between the two countries in a friendly manner at any time.

No Territorial Disputes 50

While there are no territorial disputes between France and Germany, most current issues are European in nature. Without the involvement of all related countries and the League of Nations, there is little hope for resolution, as can be seen in the opinions expressed by Prime Minister Hitler. The memorandum concludes by stating that all issues can be resolved through mutual understanding. Germany's withdrawal from Geneva is not only detrimental to Germany itself but also hinders international cooperation. It is strongly urged that Germany continue to cooperate with all nations within the scope of policies most conducive to international cooperation, which refers to the League of Nations. (Havas News Agency, 1st)

British Memorandum as a Basis for Discussion 51

Rome Expresses Satisfaction

The United States Remains Noncommittal

(London) The House of Commons is scheduled to debate the British disarmament memorandum on the 6th of this month. France has expressed some criticism of the memorandum, but Rome is satisfied because the views of Britain and Italy are aligned. It is reported that Italy will likely accept most of the British proposals, but it cannot agree to the abolition of the preliminary military training system in Italy. Furthermore, because the scope of the British proposals is broader than Italy's, there is considerable doubt as to whether it can be accepted by everyone with satisfaction. (Reuters, 1st)

(Washington) Under Secretary of State Phillips told the press that both Britain and Italy have expressed their views on the German armament issue. The State Department is unwilling to comment on the situation in Europe resulting from this. Britain has notified the State Department of the content of the memorandum, but the United States does not need to respond. (Havas News Agency, 1st)

(London) One section of the British memorandum to the related countries on the issue of disarmament states that Germany's return to the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference is a major condition for the establishment of a disarmament convention. Well-informed sources here criticize this passage, saying that while Germany's return to Geneva is desirable, it cannot be designated as an indispensable condition. However, the purpose of the British memorandum's concessions to Germany is to make Germany feel satisfied with the principle of equality in armaments. British officials believe that if this is done, Germany can return to Geneva. Political figures believe that the British memorandum can serve as the basis for future negotiations, regardless of whether they are a conference of major powers, a disarmament conference, or talks between countries through normal diplomatic channels, there is no reason why the British proposal cannot be used as a basis. As for the plan released by Italy, it is merely a brief explanation of the matters proposed by the Italian Prime Minister in Rome with British Foreign Secretary Simon. People here are quite silent about it. As for the new proposals put forward by the British Foreign Office, British public opinion generally agrees with them. From the perspective of the extreme right-wing in Britain, their support is because they believe that Britain's mediation this time is the last attempt. If it fails again, Britain can regain its freedom of action. (Havas News Agency, 1st)

(Berlin) The Berliner Tageblatt commented on the British memorandum and the disarmament plan released by Italy, saying that the intentions of Britain and Italy may be to prevent the interruption of disarmament negotiations. If France and Germany cannot reach an agreement through separate negotiations, France is eager to move the discussion of disarmament back to Geneva. The newspaper also said that the actions of Britain and Italy are indeed satisfactory because the disarmament negotiations will continue without interruption. The Politisch-Diplomatische Korrespondenz compared the optimistic attitude of Britain with the practical mentality of Italy. Britain still hopes to engage in disarmament on a small scale, while Italy regards the unwillingness of some countries to disarm as a difficult problem to solve and believes that this matter cannot be ignored. (Havas News Agency, 1st)

Japanese Budget General Meeting Questions Manchuria Problem 54

Resident Manchuria Agencies Temporarily Maintain the "Three-in-One" System

Miyakoshi Criticizes the Military's Interference in Politics, Leaving the System in Tatters

(Tokyo) The House of Representatives Budget General Meeting reopened at 1:50 PM today, starting with questions from Ikeda Hideo (Minseito Party):

Question:

Now that "Manchukuo" has realized its constitutional monarchy, Japan should strengthen its agencies in Manchuria to match the name and reality. The current "three-in-one" system is only a temporary measure for personnel relations and government actions. Is there any intention to change it in the future?

Prime Minister Saito Answer:

The current "three-in-one" system is indeed temporary, but the time for its immediate change has not yet arrived.

Ikeda Asked:

It has been repeatedly heard that there is a saying to transfer the railway affiliated land of South Manchuria Railway to "Manchukuo." I think it is not a matter that can be transferred. What is the view of the authorities?

Prime Minister Saito Answer:

The issue has not yet occurred within the government, but I also share the same feeling as you.

Ikeda Asked Again:

The commander of the army concurrently serves as the ambassador to Manchuria, which is impossible in nature. What does the government think?

Foreign Minister Hirota Answered:

I and Mr. Ikeda have the same feeling on this matter, but from the perspective of maintaining local security, it is temporarily appropriate to maintain the status quo. (Japan United Press, 2nd)

(Tokyo) House of Representatives member Miyakoshi Nagakichi fiercely attacked the military department in the lower house this afternoon, and his questions were as follows:

Miyakoshi Asked, "What preparations does the Navy have for the Second Naval Conference in 1935?" The Minister of the Navy Answered, "It is inconvenient to answer in detail, but we must maintain a force that is sufficient to defend ourselves but not enough to attack." Miyakoshi "Soldiers must not interfere in politics. The Meiji Emperor's edict is very clear. The evils of military leaders holding power did not start today. Soldiers, taking advantage of the momentum of victory, often like to interfere in politics. If the country's future is unimaginable." The Minister of the Army Answered, "Soldiers do not interfere in politics because of victory, but politics and the military should be separated." Miyakoshi "Soldiers discussing rural issues, or military officers drafting rural reform plans, is like children playing with fire, because it is not their specialty." Minister of the Army Hayashi "The military department did not have military officers draft plans." Miyakoshi "How about issuing a document clearly ordering soldiers not to discuss politics?" Minister of the Navy "Order the Education Bureau to prepare this matter, and it will be implemented soon." Miyakoshi "Former Minister of the Army Araki's participation in internal affairs meetings easily leads the people to mistakenly believe that soldiers are participating in politics. Please the military ministers be self-respecting in the future." (China United Press, 2nd)

Minister of the Army Hayashi's Reply Eases the Anti-Military Sentiment Regarding Military Discipline 55

(Tokyo) The replies of Minister of the Army Hayashi in this Diet session have attracted much attention from all parties because his wording is straightforward and full of sincerity. At the budget general meeting on the 1st, Hatta Sokichi of the Seiyukai Party first mentioned the problem of separation between the military and the people and asked Minister Hayashi to answer. The following is an excerpt from the Diet's verbatim record, summarizing the main points of the Minister's reply as follows:

Today's world situation is said to be an extraordinary period, and the stimulation it receives is unprecedented. During the Sino-Japanese War and the Russo-Japanese War, we also had a full taste of it, but the mental stimulation received by soldiers at that time is worlds apart compared to today. Although Japan's national polity has not yet been shaken, communist ideas are infiltrating it with extraordinary momentum, which can be said to be an extreme stimulation. From this perspective, the concern for the world is unusually fierce, which is the situation today. Therefore, the spray of his anger flies to the government. Therefore, we should not abandon the root and seek the branch in suppressing his thoughts. The dignity of military discipline should be maintained, but on the one hand, we should also study measures to deal with the current world situation. What should be stopped should be stopped, and we must not only stop what can be stopped. Military discipline is by no means an easy task, but the military department has not deliberately targeted political parties and fought with them, and there is no such intention. In the current situation, both the military and the people should cooperate to overcome the difficulties. In the future, we should strive to control military affairs, and at the same time, we also hope that you will make full efforts from the political standpoint. (Japan United Press, 2nd)

Tsumura Rebukes the Military Department's Rash Interference in the South Manchuria Railway at the Upper House Plenary Session 56

Japanese Army Invents Charcoal Car 61

Actively Researching Industrialization

To Make Up for the Shortage of Fuel

Preparing to Set Up Salt Companies in Manchuria to Manufacture Raw Materials for Poison Gas

(Tokyo) In order to make up for the lack of kerosene, the Tokyo Army Automobile School has been actively researching fuels to replace kerosene for years. Recently, it has invented the gasification of water charcoal and uses this charcoal gas instead of kerosene to run the engine. The school has tested it on military vehicles, and the results are quite good, and the cost can be saved by 20% compared to kerosene. In this year's budget for national fuel policy of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, a special appropriation was made to enable the school to manufacture charcoal gas vehicles, with a subsidy of 300 yen per vehicle, and it is planned to continue the subsidy for five years. On the other hand, further research will be carried out to encourage capitalists to manufacture this type of vehicle on a large scale for transportation and national defense. (China United Press, 2nd)

(Tokyo) The Japanese military department and the Ministry of Colonial Affairs want to establish salt field companies in Manchuria to actively manufacture salt as raw materials for the chemical industry. Salt is the primary raw material for poison gas bombs, and the military department is particularly keen on it. The Ministry of Colonial Affairs has agreed with capitalists on a plan to first send capitalists to the field with technicians to investigate. After they return to the country, the method of opening the business will be decided. (China United Press, 2nd)

Marley Leaves England for the United States to Report the Truth of the Japanese Attack in the Far East 62

(London) Before leaving here for the United States, Lord Marley, chairman of the Rescue Committee for Victims of German Fascism, told a reporter from Pravda that he wanted to report the horrors of German Fascism and the war crisis in the Far East to New York, Chicago, Washington, Los Angeles, San Francisco, and other American cities. Marley further pointed out that the Chinese people are the most enthusiastic sympathizers of the Soviet Union. He was always able to observe this during his stay in China. The Japanese warlords' attack on the Soviet Union cannot be successful, because the Soviet Union is strong, and at the same time, the Chinese people will ultimately help the Soviet Union. Roosevelt Holds Great Hopes for Devaluing the Yuan 64

Expanding Credit to Stabilize Market Prices

Developing American Foreign Trade

Appointing Experts to Assist in the Management of Funds

Establishing Lending Institutions to Promote Commerce

(Washington) The US House of Representatives today unanimously passed a bill to appoint ten exchange experts to assist Secretary of the Treasury Morgenthau in managing the exchange fund. President Roosevelt's reduction of the value of the US dollar to 59.06 cents has no immediate impact on various industries in the country, but the authorities have great hopes for this move: (1) expanding credit, (2) stabilizing market prices, and (3) protecting American foreign markets. At present, the French exchange rate has fallen. According to the current fixed exchange rate in the United States, it is enough to make the cash of the National Bank of France gradually flow out of the country. The United States is now engaged in foreign exchange transactions, but the outside world does not understand it very well. According to general observations, the new monetary system in the United States is a disguised "gold standard." The United States maintains its gold value at 59.06 cents and pays all international debts in cash at the fixed price in the United States. Therefore, the purpose of devaluing the US dollar is to promote the gradual stabilization of currencies in various countries. At present, France, the Netherlands, Poland, Belgium, Switzerland, and the United States all have new gold standards. Italy is making every effort to adjust its currency and also has the potential to restore the gold standard. (National News Agency, 1st)

(Washington) President Roosevelt is preparing to establish an agency to lend to exporters in order to promote exports. The lending procedures will be introduced by the Finance Rehabilitation Bank. Exporters who are currently conducting business negotiations with the United States, such as South American countries, Soviet Russia, and Balkan countries, can especially enjoy the benefits of lending. (Havas News Agency, 1st)

Affecting World Exchange Rates 65

But the Pound Sterling Remains Unshaken

The Netherlands Decides to Maintain the Gold Standard

Japanese Gold Tends to Flow into Manchuria

(New York) The pound sterling was able to resist all kinds of attacks, both real and imagined, today without being shaken at all. The foreign exchange market is chaotic, but the pound sterling remains stable. The US dollar has not fallen in value compared to gold coins, and a considerable difference in cash is still required for London and French francs, so private imports of gold can be quite profitable. The stock exchange traded 4.6 million shares, which is unprecedented since 1933. The market conditions for government bonds and goods are both stable and firm. (Reuters, 1st)

Amsterdam People here believe that the temporary stability of the US dollar is a sign that currencies are gradually returning to their new stable position. It is reported that the Dutch bank does not want to change its gold policy and will continue to ensure that there is no shortage of gold when the exchange rate requires gold. (Reuters, 10th)

(Tokyo) As a result of the deliberations by the Suio-Kai, a gold production industry group, on countermeasures against the devaluation of the US dollar, the city has already seen sales of gold at 12.20 yen per ryo (unit) and purchases at 11.65 yen due to the devaluation of the US dollar. As a result, gold production stocks skyrocketed, and the gold market also showed a firm trend. The gold purchase price of the Central Bank of "Manchukuo" is 2.95 Manchukuo yuan per gram, which translates to 11.052 Manchukuo yuan per ryo. When converted to Japanese yen, it is 12.152 yen per ryo, which is much higher than the Ministry of Finance's purchase price of 9.90 yen, and there is a gradual tendency to secretly import gold into "Manchukuo". In view of this, the conclusion was reached that the Ministry of Finance must decisively increase the price of gold, so it was decided to request the Ministry of Finance to do so. (Den-tsu Agency, 2nd)

Rumors of France Banning Gold Exports 66

(Paris) There are rumors that France is currently considering temporarily banning the export of gold, but people here do not believe it at all. It is said that the French government's policy is still to maintain the gold standard. At the same time, those who withdraw gold from the Bank of France and transfer it to London and New York are still continuing without interruption. According to financial circles, it is estimated that a total of 500 million francs were withdrawn yesterday. However, the Bank of France's gold reserves still have as much as 7.7 trillion. It is generally believed that the demand for the US dollar will not last long, and that increasing the bank interest rate to increase the cost of purchasing gold will be the first protection plan, which is undoubtedly the case. (Reuters, 2nd)

British-American Monetary Talks in Progress 67

(Washington) According to responsible sources today, informal talks between Britain and the United States on currency are currently in progress or about to begin. Officials admit that if France bans the export of gold, President Roosevelt's policy will be hindered. The foreign reaction to the new US dollar is not very satisfactory in the eyes of Americans. The general idea is that it is better to have a truce in currency than to see Britain manipulate the US dollar market, leading to a currency war. (Reuters, 2nd)

US Treasury Secretary Comments on Monetary Status 68

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau commented on the currency status, saying that the United States currently has a gold bullion standard from 1934. As for whether the Treasury Department entrusting the New York Federal Reserve Bank to buy gold is a solution to the global ban on gold exports, he declined to comment. At the request of the Treasury Secretary, the House Appropriations Committee has approved the hiring of ten experts to assist in the use of the equalization fund for the purchase of gold. Officials stipulate that pure gold is 0.899 fineness, or gold that is normally used to settle international debts and has marks indicating weight and source. (Reuters, 1st)

Japanese Government and People Confer on London Meeting Strategy 69

Given the Disastrous Defeat of the Japanese-Indian Negotiations

Decided to Take a Vigilant Attitude Toward England

(Tokyo) Due to the upcoming opening of British-Japanese consultations in London, the Japanese government decided to convene a Japanese government and people's consultation meeting on the 2nd to determine the fundamental strategy. The people's representatives attending this meeting, given the disastrous defeat of Japan in the Japanese-Indian consultations, are determined to take a tough stance against the British side. The internally determined strategy is roughly as follows: (1) Japan completely lost the Japanese-Indian consultations. In view of the results, Japanese representatives should pay the utmost attention and vigilance to the British-Japanese consultations. (2) Taking the anti-British strategy decided by the Tokyo government and people's consultation meeting in April of last year as the center, consider the new situation after the establishment of the Japanese-Indian agreement and establish a strategy for the British-Japanese conference. (3) It seems that Britain advocates for a quantity agreement or price agreement based on the number of years before Japan banned gold exports in 1931, but Japan resolutely rejects it and demands that the quantity be based on the large export quantity in 1933. (4) Oppose agreements in third-country markets. (5) Market agreements in British colonies with tariff autonomy are not subjects of discussion. (Japan United Press, 2nd)

Sun and Ma in Standoff Near Ningxia, Jin Army Takes Over Defense of Linhe 107

Sun Army's Withdrawal from Suiyuan Completed

Jin Yan Qiu Expresses Willingness to Mediate

Sun Telegraphs Beiping Requesting Supervision of Troop Withdrawal

Beiping Correspondence: Regarding the war between the Sun and Ma armies, no telegrams have arrived in Beiping from Ningxia in the past two days, so the true situation of the war is still difficult to understand. However, according to related sources, the Sun army is still continuing to attack the Ningxia provincial capital. The two sides are in a standoff at Zhujiazhai and the Greater and Lesser Mosques outside Ningxia City, and fierce battles occur from time to time. Ma Hongkui's troops have joined forces with Zhu Shaoliang's troops to meet the attack. The rumor that Ningxia has been captured by Liu Yueting's troops of the Sun army has yet to be confirmed. Sun Dianying himself is currently commanding military affairs in Dengkou. The troops left behind in Suiyuan have completed their withdrawal. Wang Jingguo's 70th Division of the Jin army telegraphed from Suiyuan today that they have taken over the defense of Linhe. For the sake of the overall situation in the Northwest, the Central Government, in addition to relieving Sun of his concurrent position as the Commissioner of Northwest Reclamation, has also decided on measures to handle the situation and telegraphed the Beiping military authorities to be responsible for handling it. He Yingqin, on behalf of the Chairman, previously telegraphed Sun Dianying, strictly ordering him to withdraw his troops to the area north of Dengkou and earnestly reduce their size. So far, no reply telegram has arrived in Beiping. Sun's attitude is still difficult to predict. If Sun continues to defy orders, then the only option is to take the final measure and handle it according to the Central Government's plan. According to reliable sources, the Sun army's attack on the Ningxia troops has reached its destination after days of fierce fighting. It is heard that the Central Government has decided to issue a clear order to suppress them, which may be issued within a week. At present, Beiping has telegraphed Yan Xishan to seek his consent. If the Jin side expresses its agreement, then the problem will naturally be easily resolved. At that time, the allied forces of Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai, as well as the Jin and Sui armies, can jointly attack and encircle them, and it will not be difficult for the Sun army to submit. Otherwise, Jin and Sui will temporarily take a supervisory attitude, and Beiping will still be responsible for handling it. Hou Cheng, who was ordered by He Yingqin to go to Taiyuan to meet Yan Xishan, returned to Beiping yesterday and reported the meeting with Yan to He. It is heard that Hou's trip was successful, and Yan expressed his willingness to do his best to resolve the Sun-Ma dispute, so there may be no problems in the future.

Ma Hongkui's representative in Beiping, Bai Jianmin, paid a visit to He Yingqin at 10:00 AM this morning to report and ask for instructions on everything. Ma Hongkui telegraphed the authorities repeatedly, requesting that the 17th Army of Baoding, commanded by Xu Tingyao, be quickly dispatched to Baotou to attack the rear of the Sun army, so that a miraculous effect can be achieved militarily. The authorities are currently considering it. He Yingqin sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang today, reporting on the Sun-Ma war and requesting instructions on how to handle it. Sun Dianying also sent two telegrams to Beiping tonight, addressed to Wang Shiping, the director of his office in Beiping, instructing him to visit He and request that personnel be sent to the front to supervise the troop withdrawal and inquire whether the pay had been suspended. The telegram reads as follows: (1) Dear Shiping, I have received both your telegrams. I am very grateful for General He's goodwill towards our troops. Yesterday, I received a telegram from General He saying that he has not suspended our troops' pay, but I don't know if it has been suspended after all. If it is indeed suspended, I... (illegible)... If it is not suspended, I will abide by the method of not suspending it. There is no other way except to have General He send someone here. Brother Lian has sent several telegrams to General He requesting him to send someone. I hope you will continue to request it nearby. Your brother Kuiyuan, 30th. (2) Dear Shiping, in my telegram at noon on the 30th, I instructed you to see General He and inquire whether the pay has been suspended after all. You should quickly inquire and reply by telegram. If the pay is not suspended and personnel are sent to defend, I will abide by General He's orders in everything. Not only will I obey in this matter, but I will also support General He to the end in the future. Otherwise, if the pay is cut off, we will be in a dead end. Tens of thousands of troops cannot be maintained. If there is a glimmer of hope, who would be willing to go to Liangshan to become bandits? Whether to send people or not, whether to suspend pay or not, these two things are up to General He to decide. I am extremely anxious and have a fervent desire to support General He and the country. If I cannot be trusted because of this matter, I will regret it for the rest of my life and will be unable to rest day and night. How I hope you will quickly reply by telegram. Your brother Kuiyuan, 30th. (February 1st)

Guizhou Civil War Has Been Resolved 108

He Jian Telegraphs Denial of Hunan Army Entering Guizhou

Wang Jialie Telegraphs That Setbacks Will Be Resolved

Guangzhou Correspondence: The situation in Guizhou recently broke down. Jiang Zizhen and Che Mingyi's troops in eastern Guizhou, in conjunction with a portion of Chen Quzhen's troops in western Hunan, attacked Wang Jialie's troops in the Laohushan area and fought fiercely with Bai Huizhang's division of Wang's troops for three days and nights. According to a telegram from Wang Jialie, they have repelled the troops. It is recently heard that Li Zongren of Guangxi Province is now actively mediating, and at the same time, he has reported to the Southwest Political Affairs Council and issued orders to all parties to stop the situation. At present, the Southwest authorities have sent Wu Houan, Miao Ruoxu, and Liu Qingnan to Guizhou to urge Mao Guangxiang to come to Guangdong. On the one hand, they have stopped military operations in Guizhou, and on the other hand, they are urging Wang to assist in Southwest political affairs in order to achieve a grand consolidation of the Southwest. At the same time, they have telegraphed He Jian of Hunan Province, requesting him to stop Chen's division in western Hunan from getting involved in the Guizhou war. He of Hunan replied yesterday by telegram, "I have respectfully received your telegram. Chen (Quzhen)'s troops in Fenghuang have been stationed in western Hunan to defend and intercept bandits. Whether they have colluded with the two divisions of Jiang (Pixu) and Che (Mingyi) to plot something and whether they have crossed the border into Guizhou this time to fuel the chaos in Guizhou, I will immediately order them to stop and investigate the truth in order to solidify our friendship between Hunan and Guizhou. Respectfully reported, He Jian, sealed." Recently, Zhang, a representative of He Jian, said that the Hunan army has always taken safeguarding the territory and pacifying the people as its duty, and defending the border. It is not yet known whether Chen's division clashed with the Guizhou army due to a misunderstanding. As for the claim that Chen Quzhen's troops have joined forces with the Jiang and Che of the Guizhou army, the Hunan army will definitely not do so, given the relationship of friendship between neighbors. With the mediation of various parties, the situation in Guizhou is now easing. Wang Jialie telegraphed on the 23rd, saying, "Since the representatives of Guangdong, Guangxi, Sichuan, and Yunnan provinces have mediated the situation in Guizhou, peace has been achieved. The overall situation here is exceptionally stable, and I am very optimistic about the future. Chen Quzhen, commander of the Hunan division, once invaded eastern Guizhou a few days ago. After my army's division commander Bai Huizhang sent troops to meet the attack, Chen's troops have retreated to their original defense in Fenghuang. We are now sending personnel to Hunan to explain and strengthen friendship with the neighboring province. This kind of small setback is not difficult to resolve. Please inform the Southwest authorities for verification." According to this, the disputes in Guizhou may be resolved within days. (Dispatch from the 29th of the 1st)

Journey of the Sichuan-Kang Expedition Group to Chongqing 109

— Lixing

Westward Journey from Shashi, Facing Perilous Rapids and Shoals

On the morning of January 26th, the boat departed Yichang, passing through the Xiling Gorge and arriving at Kongcang. This area has many submerged reefs, and the boat maneuvered windingly to avoid them. The most treacherous spot could barely accommodate one boat. The river pilot proceeded with utmost caution, as even a slight mistake could lead to capsizing. Next came Xintan, where the water current was incredibly rapid, estimated at over fifteen miles per hour. This natural water force could have been utilized to generate electricity but instead obstructed navigation. If the boat's engine power couldn't overcome the current, they had to rely on residents along the shore to pull them upstream with massive ropes. The residents considered the fees from this tow-rope labor as their sole income, knowing nothing else. Thus, this endowed wealth was merely a means for the shipping company and the residents to regulate poverty and wealth.

In the afternoon, we entered the Wu Gorge, not exiting until evening. The boat drifted along, turning with the current, with no direction in sight. A single whistle blast echoed all around. Imagining the ancients mooring their small boats along the cliffs at night, with the bright moon, monkey cries, and the sound of the water, one cannot help but feel a sense of desolation. "The Wu Gorge in Badong's Three Gorges is long, with three monkey cries, tears wet the gown." This kind of scenery was a truthful depiction in those days. Even now, traveling by steamer and experiencing it firsthand, one still struggles to grasp the feeling fully. Times are different, and so are the perceptions. In the evening, we rested at Wushan County. County Magistrate Ma Siliang came aboard to meet us, and we learned about the county's general situation. The politics and finances were the same as in other places. The mineral resources were abundant, and the produced anthracite was of good quality but had no sales channels. Wushan has the Goddess Temple of Gaotang Mountain, but it is a dilapidated temple on an earthen hill, offering nothing of interest.

On the 27th, we passed through the Qutang Gorge, Yan Yu Heap, Eight Trigrams Formation, and White Emperor City. The magnificent scenery was exhilarating. That evening, we arrived at Wanxian. The city is built against the mountain, the park is splendid, and a stone bridge spans the valley, creating a spectacular view. We arrived at the shore at dusk. We visited the leader of the tung oil industry but did not meet him. We hurriedly returned to the boat. White mist filled the river, and the moonlight was bright. Suddenly, I realized that tonight was the eve of January 28th [Shanghai Incident], and the white mist over the river resembled battle smoke in my eyes.

On the 28th, we passed through Zhongxian, the hometown of Qin Liangyu, and Fengdu, the origin of myths. We anchored at Tangliang Stone for the night. The next morning, we passed through Fuzhou and reached Chongqing. From now on, we will delve deep into the interior of Sichuan Province. (Sent from Chongqing on January 30th)

Attached is a report from the Guowen News Agency: The "Minzhu" steamer, carrying the Shanghai journalists' Sichuan-Kang Expedition Group, arrived at Shashi at 2 PM on the 23rd. Due to refueling, there was a two-hour stop. The reporters disembarked for a cursory tour of the city, which belongs to Jiangling County, the Jingzhou where Guan Zhuangmu was stationed in the Three Kingdoms, controlling the key points of Chu, Shu, Xiang, and Long, and a strategic point for military strategists. Shashi was originally a sand deposit formed by the Yangtze River, about fifteen miles from Jiangling. Because it is located on the riverbank and is a key point in the communication between Sichuan and Hubei, the municipal facilities have made considerable progress. However, due to the impact of the collapse of the rural economy, commerce is very depressed. Most residents rely on the Yangtze River for a living, and their lives are simple. The dumping of foreign goods in the area is significant, and foreign advertisements are everywhere. There are very few domestic industrial products for daily use to be found. At about 4 PM, refueling was completed, and the anchor was raised. After traveling for dozens of miles, due to darkness and shallow water, we dared not sail at night, so we stopped the boat for the night. We set off again on the morning of the 24th and arrived at Yichang at about 6 PM that afternoon. Yichang is the first gateway to enter and exit Sichuan and Hubei, so the market is still lively. However, the purchasing power of the people does not seem to be strong. Perhaps it is also affected by the bankruptcy of the rural economy. Moreover, the dumping of foreign goods is even more severe than in Shashi, and strictly speaking, the municipal facilities seem to be inferior to those of Shashi. The "Minzhu" steamer had many procedures for unloading cargo, reporting inspections, and customs duties, etc. On the 25th, it was unable to set off. It only sailed west again on the morning of the 26th. Before long, we passed Ping Shan Ba, and entered the dangerous area of the Three Gorges between Sichuan and Hubei. The details of the Three Gorges are described below: From Ping Shan Ba in Hubei to Guandukou, it is generally called Xiling Gorge, with Huangniu Gorge, Otter Creek Shoal, Kongling Shoal, Xintan, Zhucang Gorge, Niugan Mafei Gorge, Xietan, Shimen Shoal, and Niukou Shoal. From Guandukou to Wushan, it is generally called Wu Gorge, with Mother Chicken Shoal, Twelve Peaks of Wushan, Golden Helmet Gorge, Silver Armor Gorge, General Shoal, Xiatan Shoal, and Baozi Shoal. From Tielan to Yan Yu Heap, it is generally called Qutang Gorge, which includes Tie Shoal, Black Stone Shoal, Fengxiang Gorge, Shiban Jia, and Yan Yu Heap. The above are all famous dangerous places, and there are countless other rapids and submerged reefs. Everything depends on the rich experience of the pilot to maneuver and avoid them.

That morning, the boat passed Ping Shan Ba and entered the midst of ten thousand mountains. Winding and twisting, the river flowed rapidly, circling with the mountain terrain on both sides, with layers of whirlpools and myriad dangers. On both sides, the high mountains stretched continuously, piercing the clouds and veiled in morning mist and lingering clouds, making it difficult to distinguish between mountains and clouds. Passing the Kongcang Shoal, with shallow water in spring and winter, rocks stood in the center of the river, their shapes ferocious. According to Chief Officer Lei on the boat, more than four boats have sunk here. At around 10 AM, we passed Niugan Mafei Gorge. On the cliffs standing beside the river, two rocks protruded, dividing evenly on the left and right, one shaped like a cow's liver, and the other like a horse's lung, both extremely lifelike. Just as we were admiring them in amazement, the boat reached Xintan. The water was raging, surging and turbulent, with a sound like thousands of troops and horses. The "Minzhu" steamer exerted all its strength, running at full power, to fight against the current. Eventually, the chimney turned red, and the raging fire still could not overcome the pressure of the water, and there was even a tendency to retreat. The ship owner and chief officer, seeing the situation was not good, frantically blew the whistle, and had no choice but to ask for help from the local people on both banks who relied on towing boats for a living. The current here was so rapid and swirling that a goose feather could sink to the bottom of the river. If accidentally crushed by the water, the entire boat could capsize and sink into the whirlpool. The method was to throw a lead rope to the shore. The local people who gathered upon hearing the sound caught the rope, struck it against the huge rocks, and worked hard to pull. The "Minzhu" steamer, in extreme danger, was able to use this help to sail through this stormy sea. After the towing was completed, the fee paid was more than two hundred yuan. Before long, the "Minxian" steamer of the Minsheng Company also arrived, and also asked them to do the same, charging the same amount. This is also a special livelihood for the local people on the river bank. After the boat traveled a little further, it passed Zigui, the hometown of Wang Zhaojun, and then passed Badong, a border county of Hubei Province, and the journey of Xiling Gorge came to an end. Continuing west, entering the border between Sichuan and Shu, the Twelve Peaks of Wushan came into view. Since the navigation of large ships on the Yangtze River, the sound of monkeys on both banks has been silent for a long time. According to the people of Shu, no trace of monkeys has been seen. At about 5 PM in the evening, because the coal was used up, we could not reach Kuifu, so we anchored at Wushan for the night. The reporter hired a sampan to go ashore, traveled six miles, climbed Yangtai Mountain, and climbed more than a hundred stone steps to reach Wushan County. This county is located in the easternmost part of Sichuan and the northern part of Hunan. Because the land is barren and the people are poor, the county town is desolate and the people's lives are simple beyond description. The reporter toured the city in the dim twilight. The county town is broad, spanning three to four miles, with few residents. The commercial situation is beyond discussion. We passed a popular education center converted from an abandoned courtyard, with the wooden doors tightly closed, making it impossible to enter. We passed Chongfeng Temple, and visited the police station and the militia defense office in the county, but we could not find the person in charge. Initially, we wanted to go to the county government, but we were afraid of the same result as the police station, so we went down the mountain and returned to the boat. We also did not have time to visit the famous Goddess Temple of Wushan. When we returned to the boat, County Magistrate Ma Siliang of Wushan County came to welcome us. We briefly discussed the various conditions of the county as follows: The county has a total area of more than 500 li, 120 li from east to west, and 300 li from north to south, bordering Badong in Hubei Province. The total population of the county is 220,000, mostly tenant farmers. All self-cultivating farmers have been displaced due to the increasingly bankrupt economy. The annual output of grain is 200,000 to 300,000 dan. Farmers do not eat rice due to heavy taxes and difficult times, and instead eat other foods. The other products include corn, sweet potatoes, and potatoes. The production of tallow can be used to make candles, the production of pears is worth 40,000 yuan a year, and the production of plums is worth 10,000 yuan. The county is mostly mountainous, with silver, copper, iron, and coal mines. The iron ore accounts for 60 percent, but due to lack of funds and mining methods, it is still abandoned on the ground. Occasionally, some people take it using traditional methods, but the effect is very small. Recently, a few guest residents have been panning for gold in Wushan County, and they can get one or two fen of gold a day. The education funding is about 15,000 yuan a year, allocated from the slaughter tax. There are three elementary schools for boys and girls, and the girls' elementary school has a normal class with only eight students. There are 33 elementary schools in the county's 33 townships. The county government's expenses are 539 yuan per month, the county judiciary is 100 yuan per month, and other items are not easy to calculate. According to County Magistrate Ma, the police station and the militia defense are just hanging a sign. The people of the county have the bad habit of uncles marrying nieces and elder brothers marrying younger sisters, which is considered a matter of course. The border area of neighboring Hubei Province has more men than women, and they often cross the mountains to marry women by force. This is also the misfortune of Wushan women.

At dawn on the 27th, the "Minzhu" steamer roared, echoing in the mountains, leaving Wushan Gorge and heading for the shoals of Qutang Gorge. Passing White Emperor City, the place where Liu Xianzhu entrusted his orphans, the mountains stand majestically, and the river roars. One can imagine the scene of the monarchs vying for power. The old city on the hillside is magnificent, with a foreign-style building next to it, the former residence of General Wu Ziyu, who kept a low profile and lived in seclusion. Beyond this is the water and land Eight Trigrams Formation laid out by Zhuge Wuhou. The water Eight Trigrams is a huge rock shaped like a ferocious beast, standing majestically in the center of the river. The land Eight Trigrams cannot be found. While reminiscing, the boat passed Kuizhou, the leading town at the head of Sichuan and Shu. It is a pity that we did not disembark and could not visit. Before long, we passed Yunyang, and there was a Temple of Marquis Huan on the river, with a magnificent atmosphere. The notorious and dangerous Yanyu He Qutang Gorge was safely crossed while admiring the scenery and reminiscing about the ancients. It was only felt that since entering Sichuan, because the river flow was rapid, the boat exhausted all its strength to travel against the current, so the hull shook from side to side, like sailing at sea. Moreover, the climate in Sichuan is much warmer than in the lower Yangtze provinces, and the mountains on both sides have long been green. The reporter left in a hurry and was wearing winter clothes, which was unbearable.

At 6 PM that night, we arrived at Wanxian and anchored. We hired a sampan to go ashore. The entire city is built on the hillside, and its terrain is very high. It takes hundreds of steps to climb up. The city is also winding and sloping due to the mountain terrain. Sitting in a rickshaw, it feels like going up and down bridges from time to time, making it very dangerous. Wanxian has been stationed in by Sichuan general Yang Sen for the longest time. This gentleman strives for reform and works hard to build. The roads in the city are wide and the municipal administration is novel. In particular, the Wan'an Bridge cost hundreds of thousands of yuan, and it is strong, wide, and flat, no less than the modern bridges in large cities. Citizens come and go in a lively manner, and commerce is still prosperous. There is only one thing worth mentioning. The currency system here is also very complicated. One silver coin can be exchanged for more than 800 copper coins, including the dangnian, dangwushi, and diaopiao. Moreover, because copper coins are becoming cheaper every day, there is a risk that they cannot be exchanged anywhere. The Shanghai banknotes and Hubei silver coins that the reporter brought with him are not commonly used in Wanxian. It is said that the currency system is different and not commonly used every dozens of miles in Sichuan Province. The reporter was discouraged by this. Since we traveled west, we have been using dangnian copper coins at a rate of more than 600 yuan in Hankou, and we already felt unaccustomed to it. We did not expect that the currency situation in Shashi, Yichang, Wushan, and Wanxian would get worse and worse. Tung oil produced in Sichuan is the main export commodity in Wanxian, and this place is an important commercial port for export. The Zhongyuan Company controls the bulk of tung oil exports. The reporter visited Mr. Dan, the manager of the company, but Mr. Dan was resting at home due to a minor illness and could not meet him. We entrusted the company's staff to convey our sincerity and planned to visit him again on the way back to Shanghai via Wanxian to inquire about the overall situation of the tung oil export industry in Sichuan, as well as the national and international trade situation of the tung oil industry, which only Mr. Dan knows best. Because we arrived late, we did not have time to visit public and private organizations and groups, and the "Minzhu" steamer was scheduled to set sail early on the morning of the 28th, so we quickly returned to the boat after touring Wan City. The Wan City Park, which is one of the best in the Yangtze River Basin, has been famous for a long time, but we did not have time to visit it due to time constraints. In short, the reconstruction and construction of the county after being bombed by British warships is commendable.

In the early morning of the 28th, we left Wanxian in a misty fog. The dangerous shoals of the Three Gorges have all been crossed. There are occasional rapids here, but there is little danger, so the boat sped up. At noon, we passed Zhongxian, the hometown of Qin Liangyu, a female hero who resisted the bandit Zhang Xianzhong at the end of the Ming Dynasty. At 5 PM in the afternoon, we passed Fengdu. The people of this county are particularly superstitious. There are 108 temples in the county, all of which are statues of the gods of the underworld. The so-called "road guide" is sold in the temples, which is placed in the coffin of the deceased, saying that the soul can pass through the passes and mountains without hindrance. They also divide the yin and yang realms, and the people all live in the yang realm, and there are no residents in the yin realm. Their stupidity is pitiful and ridiculous. Unfortunately, the boat passed Fengdu without stopping, and it is a pity that we could not go ashore to see the strange shapes there. After traveling dozens of miles further, we anchored for the night because it was late and dark.

On the morning of the 29th, the mountain miasma shrouded the Yangtze River, and the sky turned dark and cold. The boat sailed with oars. At noon, we passed Fuzhou, but we did not stop. After dinner, we packed our luggage, and the boat arrived in Chongqing at 5 PM.

Original Text of the Proposal to Control National Grain 110

Beijing News: During the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee, committee members Liu Zhi, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Lifu, and Zhou Qigang proposed to control the nation's grain supply to promote rural recovery. They also drafted a detailed plan, which was submitted to and approved by the 393rd Central Political Conference. It was then handed over to the National Economic Committee. The original text of the proposal and plan are recorded below: "Reasons": Upon thorough examination of the current state of our nation, only two things are apparent: bandits causing turmoil and foreign powers encroaching, threatening the very existence of the nation; agriculture is in ruins, lands are desolate, even those lands that are not desolate are near ruin, rural areas are depopulated, and refugees flood the roads; the virtuous are without means, while the wicked prosper, causing morality to decline and livelihoods to be lost, making the nation unsustainable. Considering these two points, it can be said that domestic worries and foreign troubles, national crises and tribal dangers, have all reached their extremes. Those who provide relief mostly advocate suppressing bandits and resisting foreign aggression simultaneously, which is considered the best approach. However, it is not known that bandits are also people. Who would risk their lives if they were not driven by hunger and cold? When foreign aggression comes, without adequate accumulation of resources and education, merely engaging in intermittent resistance will likely yield little hope of success. Those with insight consider the restoration of rural areas as a matter of urgency, which is indeed a fitting remedy. The revival of rural areas will not only quell banditry but also lay the foundation for wealth and strength. What internal and external troubles are worth mentioning? However, this matter is of great importance. How to ensure that the people have enough food, how to alleviate the economic pressure on grain, how to harmonize grain prices, how to increase grain production, how to improve the quality of grain, how to enable people to live and work in peace, and how to allow people to recuperate, all require national planning, central coordination, and a comprehensive system with meticulous measures, as well as grand strategies that are broadly applicable. Piecemeal policies that address only the immediate problems will not be sufficient for this important task. I have drafted a brief outline of measures to control national grain based on my limited observations, hoping to contribute to the discussion. Whether it is appropriate or not is up for public deliberation. "Measures": (1) Organization: A National Grain Control Committee will be established in the capital, with three departments: management, technology, and training, responsible for administrative technology and training related to grain control. Each provincial capital will establish a Grain Control Committee for that province, directly subordinate to the National Grain Control Committee, with three departments: management, technology, and training. The management department will then establish branches in each county and city, as well as agricultural warehouses in each district. The technology department will then establish seven organizations: rice and wheat fields, miscellaneous grain fields, an insect bureau, an agricultural implements manufacturing plant, a soil survey institute, a fertilizer management office, and a collective farm. The training department will then establish three organizations: a rural cooperative training institute, an agricultural training institute, and a warehouse management training institute. Each department of the National Grain Control Committee will also do the same when necessary. (2) Tasks: The tasks of the Control Committee are: 1. To plan and organize national or provincial grain control matters; 2. To promulgate national or provincial laws and regulations regarding grain control; 3. To promote cooperatives and cooperative warehouses for grain transportation, sales, consumption, and storage; 4. To determine the quantity of grain storage, transportation, sales, and distribution in various places; 5. To determine the quantity of grain to be bought and sold externally; 6. To raise funds to regulate grain prices. The tasks of the Management Department are: 1. To implement various resolutions of the Control Committee; 2. To guide and supervise the investigation and statistics of grain nationwide or province-wide; 3. To guide the registration of grain harvests and imports and exports nationwide or province-wide; 4. To establish and manage agricultural warehouses; 5. To guide, promote, and supervise cooperatives and cooperative warehouses for grain transportation, sales, consumption, and storage. The tasks of the Technology Department are: 1. To implement various resolutions of the Control Committee regarding the improvement of grain production technology; 2. To research methods to increase grain production and improve quality; 3. To design the construction of new-style warehouses; 4. To research methods to conserve grain consumption. The tasks of the Training Department are: 1. To increase farmers' knowledge and skills in farming; 2. To increase farmers' knowledge of rural organizations; 3. To increase farmers' true spirit of mutual assistance; 4. To enable farmers to reform bad customs in rural areas; 5. To enable farmers to understand the benefits and methods of various agricultural cooperatives; 6. To train warehouse management personnel. The tasks of each county and city branch are: 1. To handle grain control matters within the jurisdiction according to the orders of the provincial management department; 2. To investigate and statistically count the population and grain consumption within the jurisdiction; 3. To investigate and statistically count the amount of grain stored within the jurisdiction; 4. To register grain harvests or imports and exports and market information within the jurisdiction; 5. To determine the quantity of grain storage, transportation, sales, and distribution in each district; 6. To supervise grain prices within the jurisdiction and crack down on unscrupulous merchants who monopolize, manipulate, adulterate, and mix grain; 7. To promote and supervise cooperatives and cooperative warehouses for grain transportation, sales, consumption, and storage within the jurisdiction; 8. To investigate and statistically count the grain disaster situation and the causes of famine within the jurisdiction; 9. To raise funds to regulate grain prices within the jurisdiction; 10. To inspect the grade of grain within the jurisdiction. The tasks of the district agricultural warehouse are: 1. To ensure the stability of the agricultural market; 2. To ensure the circulation of agricultural finance; 3. To concentrate grain; 4. To apply various scientific methods to manage grain storage; 5. To promote grain transportation and sales cooperatives and consumer cooperatives. The rice and wheat fields will select rice and wheat varieties that are abundant in yield and resistant to pests and diseases, and after improving their cultivation methods, they will be promoted to farmers. The miscellaneous grain fields will select miscellaneous grain varieties that are abundant in yield and resistant to pests and diseases, and after improving their cultivation methods, they will be promoted to farmers. The Insect Bureau will study methods to prevent and control pests and protect beneficial insects, as well as grain insecticides and equipment, and distribute them to farmers in various places. The Agricultural Implements Manufacturing Plant will research and create various suitable agricultural implements and promote them to farmers. It will also investigate the old and new agricultural implements that require less effort and yield more results, and imitate or improve them, so that they are fully applicable to the agricultural conditions of each area before promoting them to farmers. The Fertilizer Management Office will conduct various experiments on ordinary crops and fertilizers, and use scientific methods to produce pure and high-quality artificial fertilizers, stipulate their application standards and methods, and promote them to farmers. It will also manage and crack down on artificial fertilizers that are adulterated and harmful to farmland. The Soil Survey Institute will conduct investigations and statistics on various types of soil in various places, and study methods to improve them and promote them to farmers. The Collective Farm will apply scientific theories, methods, and equipment to carry out large-scale land reclamation. The Rural Cooperative Training Institute will teach farmers the theories, benefits, and methods of various agricultural cooperatives, so that they can automatically promote various agricultural cooperatives. The Agricultural Training Institute will teach farmers various new knowledge and technologies in agriculture, forestry, silkworm breeding, and so on, so that they can apply them. The Warehouse Management Training Institute will teach people new knowledge and methods of scientific warehouse management, so that they can apply them. 3. System Table: For the sake of clarifying the entire organization of the Grain Control Committee, its system table is listed below:

National Grain Control Committee

｜Management Department

｜Technology Department

｜Grain Control Committees of each province [

Management Department {Branches in each county and city

District Agricultural Warehouse

Technology Department [

｜Rice and Wheat Fields

｜Miscellaneous Grain Fields

｜Insect Bureau

｜Agricultural Implements Manufacturing Plant

｜Fertilizer Management Office

｜Soil Survey Institute

｜Collective Farm

｜Training Department [

｜Rural Cooperative Training Institute

｜Agricultural Training Institute

｜Warehouse Management Training Institute

The above is a simple and principled construction. As for detailed and specific measures, various experts need to plan separately. (Ethnic Community News)

Wuxi 111

County Magistrate Punishes Police for Neglecting Gambling

County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, previously received reports that gambling was rampant in the 13th district, and there were inevitably people who were protecting it, so he personally went to the district on the 24th of last month and arrested a gambler named Shen Quangen in Huadafang Village, and arrested the boss Bao Zhu, gamblers Hu Jinqi, Xu Abing, and policeman Hong Zhaosheng in Jinhuyuan Teahouse in Nanqiao Town. They were taken to the county for custody, and the patrol officer Wang Xuehan of the Third Substation of the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau was ordered to bring Yuan Wangquan and Wang Zhengxiang, the owners of Jinhuyuan, to the county along with the gambling tools. Later, County Magistrate Yan sent all the people and stolen goods to the Public Security Bureau for strict punishment. Now, County Magistrate Yan believes that gambling is rampant in the district, and the Third Substation of the Eighth Branch is nearby, so it cannot shirk its responsibility. Therefore, he yesterday specifically ordered Li Wengong, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, to strictly punish the patrol officer Wang Xuehan. Liu Shide, the director of the Eighth Branch, was given a reprimand for failing to supervise properly. At the same time, Fan Jishi, the assistant member of the 13th district, was deemed to be covering up and should be replaced. He also ordered Zhu Zhengxin, the district chief of the 13th district, to strictly guard against gambling and severely punish those who neglect their duties.

Opening of the People's Maternity Hospital 112

This county was ordered to set up a People's Maternity Hospital, which has been in preparation for several months. Recently, the preparations have been completed. The hospital is located at the old site of the Labor Hospital in Baer Lane in the city. The opening ceremony was held at 10:00 AM yesterday. More than 100 people attended, including Xu Yongji, the party committee member, Yan Shenyu, the county magistrate, Jiang Zhaoju, the representative of the Department of Health of the Ministry of Internal Affairs, and Wang Yuanchen, the representative of the Department of Civil Affairs. The chairman was County Magistrate Yan. First, the chairman reported on the preparation process, and then the party committee members, department members, and guests gave speeches. The ceremony concluded at 12:00 PM. It was also heard that the hospital, in addition to obstetrics, also has a general medical clinic, which will start providing consultations today.

Jiaxing 113

Police Inspection of Hotel Dispute

On the 28th, late at night, police officers from the responsible public security station inspected the Andong Hotel in Jiaxing East Gate. They also forced the hotel to sign a guarantee and took one accountant and one tea server to the headquarters for detention. The next day, they handcuffed the two men and escorted them to the local branch court. After questioning, they were found to have no criminal suspicion and were ordered to return. Now, the Public Security Bureau believes that the case constitutes obstruction of public service and has filed a lawsuit with the court. The prosecutor's office has scheduled a hearing for the 5th to summon witnesses for questioning. The hotel, on the other hand, believes that the unwarranted detention and handcuffing of its staff constitute a violation of criminal law. They also argue that public officials abusing their power are different from ordinary criminals. They have hired lawyers to file complaints with both the judicial and administrative authorities.

Zhenjiang 114

Winter Relief Bureau Begins Distribution

The winter relief effort in the provincial capital, which began its investigation on January 16th, has finally been completed after half a month. It is now scheduled to begin distributing relief rice on February 6th, to be completed within the lunar New Year. The distribution points are: (1) Zhenjiang County Party Headquarters, Xianhe Lane, Xinximen, inside the city; (2) Cargo depot, Zhaoshang Lane, Xiaozhakou, outside the city; (3) Hours: Inside and outside the city, from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM, and from 1:00 PM to 9:00 PM. Relief rice will be distributed upon presentation of the relief investigation ticket.

Huzhou 115

Robbery Occurs in Minjiawan

In Minjiawan, Yandang Township, Wuxing Second District, a farmer named Min Senbao, who is moderately wealthy, was targeted by bandits. On the night of the 29th of last month, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived, armed with rifles and pistols, speaking with an Anhui accent. They broke down the door and ransacked the house, stealing dozens of items of clothing, over a hundred yuan in silver, and twelve carts of silk. They also beat Senbao and his son Xuan, causing injuries. Before leaving, they fired shots into several villages.

Gaoyou 116

Police and Soldiers Fight, Resulting in Death

Xu Yangmin and Li Guang'an, two police officers of the Second Squad of the Ninth District Sanlangmiao Police Department stationed in the county, had an argument yesterday (the 30th) and fought. Xu Yangmin threw a wooden stool at Li, hitting him in the vital area of the head. Li immediately fell to the ground, unconscious. He died of his injuries in the evening. The squad leader then took the assailant, Xu Yangmin, into custody. The squad leader, Shi Xingrui, was patrolling in various villages at the time, and a messenger has been dispatched to report the incident for processing.

Xiaoshan 117

Fire in Waisha Kills Two

The home of Han Youxin, a resident of Waisha, Xiaoshan West Township, caught fire on the night of the 31st due to carelessness while cooking dinner. In an instant, five two-story houses and seven single-story houses were engulfed in flames. An elderly woman in her seventies and a five-year-old child were unable to escape and were burned to death. More than ten chickens and ducks were also burned to death. The loss is estimated to be over ten thousand yuan.

Haimen 118

Red Pill Factory Robbed in Shangsanhe Town

The residence of a certain Du in Hedong, Shangsanhe Town, Second District of the West, has a red pill factory. The daily production volume is alarming, and the suffering of the people is evident. The red pill boss, Xi Guangjun, fled after being reported and exposed for manufacturing red pills at his home in Nantong Chuan Port in September of last year, and is still wanted. Now, he has secretly returned to Sanhe Town and resumed his old business. Because he is good at adapting to the environment, he has not been caught by the authorities despite the strict prohibition by the National Government. Unexpectedly, several uninvited guests carrying four box guns arrived the other night, claiming to be searching, and stole a total of eight sacks of red pills and raw materials, valued at several thousand yuan.

Jiangyin 119
