A Word to Our Valued Customers Nationwide 120

The Manufacturing of Candies From Past to Present

— Xi Guansheng

In recent years, domestic industry has transformed from purely old-fashioned methods to imitation manufacturing. Furthermore, many light industries have indeed achieved considerable success. This demonstrates that while various aspects of China have stagnated over the past twenty years, the industrial sector has shown a trend of rapid advancement.

Domestic scientific candy production is also a unit of light industry. From sesame candy to European-style candy, its color, aroma, and taste can certainly compete with imported products. This also shows the formation of a new and modern landscape, and Guanshengyuan is a contributing member. In the past decade, we have produced over a hundred types of candies. The "Top Ten Candies" are the part that we dare to be confident about. Unexpectedly, the domestic candy market dominated by foreign merchants has gradually lost its original position in recent years. This is undoubtedly the result of Chinese people's love for domestic products, which has preserved a great deal of the nation's vitality.

Now, let me tell fellow compatriots who love domestic goods about the past and present of our candy manufacturing.

The early period of the decline of old-fashioned candies was precisely when foreign candies were rampant. Countries such as England, America, and Japan were the first to import, followed by competition from other countries. The domestic market was almost entirely dominated by foreign merchants. The reason was that at that time, customs sovereignty was controlled by foreign advisors, and the import of candies was only intended to supply foreign residents in places like Tianjin and Beijing, so no one paid attention, and no taxes were levied. As a result, foreign candies were imported in large quantities. Initially, they only became popular among the aristocracy, but after several years of aggressive marketing by foreigners, they spread to the upper and middle classes in the treaty ports. At that time, based on the nationality of the candy, there were English, American, German, French, Japanese, Swiss, Dutch, and Russian candies. By type, there were all kinds imaginable. In particular, a certain country's chewing gum had the largest sales. In the face of foreign merchants competing with each other, our economic losses were undoubtedly enormous. Guanshengyuan, alerted to this crisis, began manufacturing its own candies, hoping to recover partial profits from a small starting point. Today's "Top Ten Candies" are precisely our small achievements from ten years of effort. The main conditions for candy are color, aroma, and taste. However, we confidently invite our fellow countrymen to try our candies and offer strict criticism to see if they can be compared with imported goods.

Recovering rights and interests was my initial motivation for starting manufacturing. But there are still things I can tell my fellow countrymen: (1) Mechanical equipment costs millions at every turn. It is not easy to gather such large funds in the budding stage of industry. However, most of our application equipment is self-made. Although the cost is small, the effect is the same. This is one way we have broken through difficult circumstances and practiced industrial salvation. (2) We have never had Western technicians. We rely entirely on the experience of experts returning from America and a constant attitude of research to gradually reach the intended standards. (3) The raw materials for European-style candies are mostly imported from foreign countries. In this way, although we recovered some rights on the commodity, the raw materials are still a huge loss. Therefore, in addition to what we cannot manufacture ourselves, we adopt a policy of self-sufficiency in raw materials. (4) Excellent candies should at least have (A) authentic raw materials, (B) rich nutrition, and (C) moderate sweetness. For ten years, we have never dared to relax on the above three points. At the same time, imported candies are priced incredibly high and cannot suit the purchasing power of ordinary people. However, compared to our prices, Guanshengyuan products are about 40-50% cheaper, reducing the burden on customers, which was also the initial motivation for manufacturing.

That's all I have to say. I hope that my valued customers will not hesitate to give me your guidance!

Sino-British Radio Station Opens Today 121

Zhu Jia骅 Arrives in Shanghai Early Morning to Preside

Wu Tiecheng Represents the Central Government to Deliver a Speech

According to the Central News Agency, the direct Sino-British communication organized by the International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications will hold its opening ceremony at 3:00 PM today at the Zhenru Radio Station. Minister of Communications Zhu Jiahua and his wife left Beijing last night and arrived in Shanghai this morning to serve as the chairman of the ceremony. The Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and others have all telegraphed Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng to represent them in delivering a speech. Tonight, from 6:00 PM to 8:00 PM, Minister Zhu and his wife will host the press at 80 Seymour Road to report the details. Details are as follows:

Opening Ceremony Order 122

The order of the opening ceremony is as follows: (1) Opening, (2) Everyone stands at attention, (3) Sing the Party Song, (4) Bow three times to the Prime Minister, (5) Read the Prime Minister's Will respectfully, (6) Silence, (7) Chairman's Report, (8) Speech by the Representative of the Central Party Headquarters, (9) Speech by the Representative of the National Government, (10) Speeches by Guests, (11) Opening Ceremony (Ms. Cheng Peifang, wife of Zhu Jiahua), (12) Tour of the Radio Station, (13) Photography, (14) Adjournment.

Participating Representatives 123

The Ministry of Communications has been preparing for Sino-British communication for two years, so the etiquette of the opening ceremony is extraordinarily grand. Minister Zhu Jiahua came to Shanghai from Beijing last night and arrived this morning. Zhu will serve as the chairman of the ceremony. The National Government also telegraphed Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng yesterday to represent them in delivering a speech. The Central Party Headquarters representative may also be Wu. The City Chamber of Commerce has also designated its chairman, Wang Xiaolai, to attend and deliver a speech. Other agencies have also selected representatives to attend the grand event. As for foreign guests, such as the British Consul General in Shanghai, Bailey Nan, and the chairman of the Shanghai British Chamber of Commerce, Maxwell, are all scheduled to attend and deliver speeches. All speeches can be heard by those with radios with 580 and 700 cycle wavelengths.

Venue Arrangement 124

The venue is set up on the lawn next to the radio station, with a reed shed erected. The shed can accommodate five or six hundred guests. The shed is filled with rattan chairs, arranged neatly. At the east end of the shed, a wooden platform is erected, with a portrait of the Prime Minister in the middle, flanked by the Party and national flags. The four sides are filled with the flags of various countries. The entire venue is arranged exceptionally neatly.

Vehicle Traffic 125

Guests' vehicles, if they do not have a Huajie (Chinese area) pass, can pass unhindered from 1:00 PM to 6:00 PM with a viewing invitation. The Zhabei Chinese Business Council's car will also be on display at the radio station from 1:00 PM this afternoon to benefit the public.

Construction Process 126

Wen Yuqing, Director of the International Telecommunications Bureau, published the construction process of the international radio station, saying that the 46th meeting of the Guangdong Political Branch Association on August 5, 1928, had a proposal to establish an international radio station and telegraphed the Central Political Conference to implement it. Later, in November of that year, the Construction Committee ordered four sets of Lowatt transceivers from the German Telefunken Company and two sets of 20-kilowatt transceivers from the American Associated Wireless Radio Company to build a transmitting station in Zhenru and Fenglin Bridge in Shanghai, and a receiving station in Liuhang, Baoshan. It also signed direct communication contracts between Shanghai and Manila, Shanghai and San Francisco, and Shanghai and Berlin with the Philippine Associated Wireless Radio Company, the American Associated Wireless Radio Company, and the German Berlin Marine Wireless Radio Company. Before the completion of the Zhenru and Fenglin Bridge stations, a Sino-Philippine transfer radio station was established in Shanghai, equipped with two 500-watt transmitters. On January 14, 1929, it officially communicated with Manila. In February of that year, the Ministry of Communications ordered a 15-kilowatt transceiver from the French Long-Distance Telephone Company. In April, the International Communications Large Radio Station Preparatory Office was organized, and a direct communication contract was signed between Shanghai and Paris with the French Wireless Radio Company. In August, the Ministry of Communications was ordered to unify the national wireless radio management powers, and the wireless radio business operated by the Construction Committee was taken over and merged. Base collection, construction of station buildings, roads, bridges, and installation of equipment, antennas, cables, power, and other equipment were actively carried out in Zhenru and Liuhang. In March 1930, the Fenglin Bridge transmitting station was completed. In November, the Zhenru transmitting station and the Liuhang receiving station were completed. On December 6, they officially communicated directly with European and American countries.

Expansion of Construction 127

London, England, is the world's commercial center. The telegrams between our country and London account for almost half of the foreign telegraph fees, but there is still no direct line. In June 1932, the Ministry of Communications negotiated with the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund to borrow £50,000 in British gold to order two 20-kilowatt high-energy short-wave receiving machines from the British Marconi Company, and signed a Sino-British communication contract with the London Imperial Transport Company. New buildings were added to the Zhenru transmitting station, new machines were installed, and antenna towers were added. In addition, the remote-controlled transmission aerial cables between Shanghai Zhenru and Shanghai Liuhang were easily damaged. A 50-pair underground cable was ordered from the British Xiangtai Foreign Company to be laid to ensure permanence. A backup power plant and a machine factory were set up in the Zhenru transmitting station to facilitate the acquisition of current and the repair of machines. All expansion projects were completely completed by the end of last year and were successfully tested with the United Kingdom. The opening ceremony is scheduled to be held today and officially communicated.

A Glimpse of the Radio Station 128

A reporter from the Central News Agency drove to Zhenru yesterday afternoon for a visit. He was led by the station engineer Zong Zhifa and explained everything. Two Sino-British receivers are installed after the Sino-American reporting machine. Special new houses have been added there, arranged horizontally in the middle. Each machine is divided into four parts, gradually increasing the power, and then transmitting it to the antenna for distribution. The bulb in the last part is as big as a dipper. Because the heat is too high, oil is used to adjust it to dissipate heat. At the left end of another machine, there is a live machine. According to Zong, the reporter is actively preparing for calls, and the central control room on Nanjing Road has now been opened as a broadcast room. After the ceremony tomorrow (ie today), Minister Zhu Jiahua also plans to give a broadcast speech to the United Kingdom in that room at 8:00 PM. He then went to the Sino-Philippine and Sino-French communication rooms. Each machine was similar. Later, he led to the power generation room for a visit. Although the machine has been installed, it is not usually used, because the station uses commercial electricity, and it has its own generator for backup in case of commercial electricity obstacles. Outside the power generation room, there are several lathes for repairing other parts. There are now eight antenna towers. Three were originally installed, three are newly built, and two were moved from Hangzhou and Wusong. The European beam antenna tower is directed northwest, and the American one is directed southeast. The staff dormitory is newly built on the west side of the yard. The station covers an area of more than two hundred acres, with each station building built around the perimeter, with trees planted everywhere. The scenery is quite good.

British Telegraphic Congratulations 129

After the completion of Sino-British communication, the relationship between the two countries will become perfect day by day. Therefore, British Foreign Secretary Simon specially telegraphed Wang Jingwei, who is also the Minister of Foreign Affairs, to congratulate him. He also learned that the British Minister of Posts and Telecommunications and others have telegraphed the Ministry of Communications to congratulate him.

Kong Xiangxi Talks About the Executive Yuan's Consolidation of Land Tax 133

Detailed Measures Based on Reports from Various Provinces

Director of the Unified Tax Administration Xie Qi Resigns and is Persuaded to Stay

Financial Institutions in Min Province Gradually Recover

According to the New Sound News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, has been going to the Finance Ministry Office to work and contacting all important officials since he returned to Shanghai from Beijing. A reporter from the New Sound News Agency visited Kong at his residence yesterday afternoon to discuss various matters as follows:

Consolidation of Land Tax 134

According to Kong, the land tax case submitted by the Ministry of Finance at the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee, after being passed by the congress, has been handed over to the Executive Yuan for research and handling. However, the land tax collection situation in various provinces varies from place to place. How to prudently request tax reductions and carry out consolidation still requires detailed measures based on the reports submitted by the various provinces in the past before it can be implemented. If we must conduct another investigation before holding it, I am afraid the time will be too long and it will be difficult to realize. As for the land declarations that have already been handled by various provinces and counties, in order to avoid formalities, they will not be held accountable.

Foreign Rice and Wheat 135

As for the issue of import duties on foreign rice and wheat, it was passed by the Legislative Yuan in August of last year. Later, because Minister Song attended the World Economic Conference in London, our country joined the tariff truce and it was not held. By November 16th, after our side notified the countries in the tariff truce and officially withdrew, because it would only take effect after one month, and at the same time, after I took office, all parties urged me to hold it, so it was only implemented on December 16th to save domestic agricultural products. After the announcement, Guangdong Province is still a tax-free port because both rice and wheat in Guangdong Province must rely on external supply. However, because the domestic supply and demand have not been balanced, we will continue to find ways to transport and sell rice and wheat produced in the Yangtze River area to Guangdong to balance it. The effect of saving the domestic rural economy will be even greater.

Tax Reduction Issues 136

The reporter then asked how the Ministry of Finance would deal with the request from wheat flour merchants for tax exemptions. According to him, this fact originated from the excessively high price of American wheat. It turned out that there was 10 million US dollars in American cotton and wheat loans to buy American wheat. Because the price of American wheat was too high, for example, the world wheat price was 2.56 yuan, and China was only about 2.2 yuan, but American wheat had to be 2.8 yuan, so merchants felt quite difficult. Now the United States has not agreed to reduce the price, but the Ministry of Finance, in order to be considerate of merchants, will not cause merchants to suffer excessively, and is currently in consultation.

Persuading Xie Qi to Stay 137

He also said that Xie Qi, Director of the Unified Tax Administration, requested leave because his wife was ill. Director Xie was afraid that the leave would be too long and would delay official business, so he submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Finance. However, Director Xie is very familiar with and proficient in taxation, and has an excellent reputation, so I did not approve it and decided to persuade him to stay.

Post-Disaster Work in Min Province 138

As for the tax collection institutions in Min Province, the Ministry of Finance has long sent personnel to gradually recover them and work as usual. The post-disaster expenses in Min Province are all raised by the Min Provincial Government itself, and the central government does not need to allocate funds to handle the post-disaster issues in Min Province.

Ministry of Communications Orders Both Airline Companies to Pay Attention to the Climate Between Two Locations 144

Altitude Limit Below 500 Feet, Visibility Below One Mile

No passenger flights should be made to avoid unexpected situations en route

The Ministry of Communications, in response to the accident involving a China Aviation Corporation Shanghai-Guangdong flight in November of last year, dispatched aviation experts and established a committee to study the incident. The committee concluded that climate was the cause. Therefore, the Ministry specifically instructed both Eurasia and China Aviation Corporations to stipulate flight procedures. The Ministry order is recorded as follows: Postal transport aviation values safety above all else, and examining the climate before takeoff is closely related to safety. Hereafter, on any route, between any two locations, if the altitude limit is less than 500 feet and the visibility is less than one mile, no passenger flights should be made to avoid unexpected situations en route. It is hereby ordered that the company transmit these instructions to all pilots to strictly comply with and report back to the ministry. This order.

Bureau of Commodity Inspection Changes to New System of Weights and Measures 145

Public notice posted yesterday

Three points to note

The Bureau of Commodity Inspection, in order to comply with the order to change to the new system of weights and measures, specially issued Public Notice No. 341 yesterday, stating: "According to Instruction No. 23185 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, after changing the units of quantity for commodity inspection to the new system of weights and measures, the amount of inspection fees should be converted accordingly. The Ministry is currently revising all commodity inspection fees in a comprehensive manner. To facilitate the continuation of work, before the revision of the said fees, the original amounts will continue to be charged temporarily. Aside from distribution, you are hereby ordered to comply with this order." Upon receipt of this instruction, the Bureau immediately began implementation from today. The points to note are listed below: (1) When applying for inspection, the quantities in the old system should be converted to the new system. (2) On the application form and certificate, the quantity in the new system should be written before the quantity in the old system, which should be written in parentheses. (3) Inspection fees will be temporarily charged according to the original amount. In addition to separate orders to all departments and groups to comply with, this notice is hereby issued for all merchants to take note of. This notice.

China Savings Bank Ordered to Close at the End of this Month 148

Deposits of depositors will be returned in accordance with regulations

The China Savings Bank, located at the intersection of Henan Road and Jiaotong Road, has been in existence for ten years. The main reason for its establishment was to imitate the methods of the International Savings Society, solicit depositors, and operate prize-linked savings. The fixed capital was 500,000 yuan, divided into three types of depositors: three yuan, six yuan, and twelve yuan. The top prize was 500 yuan, and the remaining prizes were handled in accordance with the methods of the International Savings Society. In the beginning, the number of depositors was quite large, but it gradually decreased. Manager Shan Yiting and the shareholders were all North China merchants. In ordinary times, they also handled current deposits and loans.

Ordered to suspend business Since its establishment, the bank has never joined the Bankers Association. Its main business was prize-linked savings. After the Qi-Lu War, it suffered a major setback. The shareholders had long intended to close down the bank. However, prize-linked savings by banks is prohibited by law. Therefore, after an investigation by the Ministry of Finance, the bank was ordered to cease operations.

Closing at the end of the month After receiving the order, the bank published a notice of closure in the newspaper on the 31st of last month and immediately began closing operations. It was originally scheduled to complete all operations in three days, but some depositors received the news later and were unable to withdraw their deposits in time. Therefore, the deadline has been extended to the end of this month. As of now, there are still more than 80 depositors, with terms of ten and six years. All deposits will be returned in accordance with regulations. Current deposits and loans also amount to tens of thousands of yuan. These were all gradually settled and repaid by the end of the lunar year.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Writes to the Whangpoo Conservancy Bureau to Dredge the Suzhou Creek Channel 150

To facilitate water transportation

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce wrote to the Whangpoo Conservancy Bureau yesterday, stating: "We are writing to you regarding a joint letter received on the 31st of this month from the rice milling industry, miscellaneous grain and oil cake industry, bean and rice industry, miscellaneous grain industry, miscellaneous grain retail industry, rice and grain sales industry, and other trade associations in this city, as well as Fuxin No. 1 Flour Mill, Jiangsu Bank Warehouse, Four Banks Joint Savings Society Warehouse, Yukang Warehouse, Shanghai Jiaotong Bank Warehouse, Lao Yongchang Coal Company, Yifeng Machinery Sawmill, Hengkang Warehouse, Taichang Kangji Firm, Xieji West Warehouse, Shanghai Guohua Bank Warehouse Department, Shengren Coal Company, Yucheng Timber Company, Yongcheng Coal Company, Deli Runyuan Bamboo Firm, Tongxingshunji Warehouse, Yixing Yuanji Foreign Warehouse, Xintong Foreign Warehouse, Yitaixing Coal Company, and Yutong Fuji Flour Mill, stating that during the winter season, when the water is low, ships are congested in the Suzhou Creek area, often blocking traffic. As a result, merchants suffer significant losses in freight. Although the Water Patrol Team maintains and clears the waterway day and night, this is a temporary solution and not a fundamental solution. Your association is the leader of the commercial community, and we would like to request that you write to the dredging engineering office of the Whangpoo Conservancy Bureau to quickly take advantage of the low water in the winter season to dredge the silted parts of the Suzhou Creek to facilitate traffic. This is our earnest plea." It has been verified that there is a large amount of siltation in the waterways of the Suzhou Creek area, and water transportation is often obstructed. Taking advantage of the low water in the winter season to dredge the silted areas is indeed a crucial step. Accordingly, we are forwarding the situation as described above, and we respectfully request that your bureau instruct the dredging engineering office to commence dredging immediately to facilitate waterway traffic. We eagerly anticipate this."

Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway Expected to Resume by the End of this Month 151

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after the completion of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway, the long-distance buses operated by the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Administration traveled from Hangzhou via Haining Zhapu to Minhang, connecting with the Shanghai-Minhang buses to Shanghai, which was convenient for travelers. In December of last year, due to military reasons and busy transportation, there were not enough vehicles allocated, so all the branch lines belonging to the route, such as Linping-Changan, Yuanhua-Pinghu, etc., were completely suspended. At the same time, the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway passenger buses were reduced to two trips up and down each day. Now, the National Economic Commission and the Highway Administration have allocated vehicles to find ways to restore the service. It is expected that the service can be fully restored to its original state by the end of this month.

Ministry of Communications Newly Revised Regulations for Reporting and Submitting Telegraph Translation Fees 152

Official telegrams with urgent classification should be marked with a fee-paying label

The Ministry of Communications has newly revised four regulations for reporting and submitting telegraph translation fees collected by each telegraph office: (1) If the translation fees collected are more than 50 yuan, they should be reported and submitted once a month. (2) If the amount is less than 50 yuan for several months, it should be reported and submitted once every three months. (3) If funds are insufficient and must be retained, prior approval should be obtained before offsetting. (4) Regardless of the amount, it must be reported separately by month for auditing purposes. In addition, the character "　" has been added to the "New Compilation of Missing Characters in Plain and Cipher Codes," with the code number 9669, and will be implemented from March 1st. In addition, the words "Urgent," "Special Urgent," etc., prefixed to the addresses of official telegrams, will be used as fee-paying labels and will be charged per word. All of the above regulations have been instructed to all telegraph stations and bureaus for implementation in accordance with the regulations.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Jiaoji Railway Sign Joint Transportation Agreement Yesterday 153

Prices to be determined and implemented on March 1st

Jiaoji Railway and other personnel sent to Austria for inspection

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is handling national water and land joint transportation. The Longhai Railway has already implemented the agreement. The Jiaoji Railway agreement was signed yesterday. The Qingdao Municipal Government and the Jiaoji Railway sent personnel to Shanghai and then to Guangdong to inspect joint transportation. The details are recorded as follows:

Agreement Signed 154

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Jiaoji Railway are conducting joint transportation on the Jiaoji Railway in accordance with the joint transportation regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Railways. The detailed rules of implementation had already been drafted by both parties, totaling eleven articles, and were written in duplicate. The Jiaoji Railway had already signed the agreement, and Sun Zhenwu, the director of the Qingdao branch of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, brought it to Shanghai. It was approved by the 56th board meeting of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Due to procedural reasons, it was delayed until yesterday, when General Manager Liu Hongsheng officially signed the agreement. The Jiaoji Railway and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company each kept a copy and submitted it to the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications for record.

Personnel Sent for Inspection 155

The Jiaoji Railway Administration specially sent Tan Shukuai, the deputy director of the Traffic Department, and Wang Xichang, the deputy director and senior consultant of the Qingdao Municipal Port Authority, from Qingdao to Shanghai last month and returned to Shanghai around the 10th of this month. At the same time, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company also sent Sun Zhenwu, the director of the Qingdao branch, to Hong Kong and Guangdong to inspect joint transportation matters on the way to Zhao'an.

Scheduled Implementation 156

The freight rates for joint transportation on the Jiaoji Railway had already been drafted by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Jiaoji Railway and were planned to be officially implemented on March 1st. However, it is necessary to wait until Tan Shukuai, Wang Xichang, and Sun Zhenwu return to Shanghai from Guangdong to discuss and decide. In general, there will be no problems. As for joint transportation matters, the Qingdao branch of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will jointly with the Jiaoji Railway set up a joint transportation office in Qingdao to handle the matters. No separate office will be established in Shanghai.

Opposition Ineffective 157

After the Jiaoji Railway was recovered from Japan by our country, Japanese merchants such as the Dalian Kisen Kaisha tried to oppose the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's handling of joint transportation, claiming that the redemption price of the Jiaoji Railway had not been paid. However, the Jiaoji Railway and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will not stop due to the opposition of Japanese merchants. It is expected that after the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company implements joint transportation on the Jiaoji Railway, private transportation companies such as Sanbei Zhengji and foreign companies such as Jardine Matheson and Taikoo Dalian will not be unable to operate, because in the future, when joint transportation is implemented, goods will be divided into two types: joint transportation and non-joint transportation.

Standing Committee Meeting of the Cooperative Enterprise in this City 158

The Cooperative Enterprise Committee of this city held its 14th standing committee meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday. Committee members Wang Zhixin (representing Miao Zizhong), Wu Juenong, Wu Huanru, Xu Yefu (representing Wang Gang), Zhang Binghui, Wang Shuji, and Hang Dingan attended. Chairman Zhang Binghui presided over the meeting and discussed that the scope of the committee's work plan last year was too broad, and due to limitations in financial and human resources, it was not possible to fully realize each item. There were shortcomings in the development of committee affairs. In order to avoid repeating the same mistakes, it was decided to focus the committee's work on a few key points and achieve them within a limited time frame in order to achieve twice the result with half the effort. The following proposals were resolved: (1) How should the committee's work be carried out this year? (Resolution) 1. Promote workers' consumer cooperation in this city. 2. Investigate the cooperative societies that have already been established in this city. 3. Provide practical guidance to the cooperative experiment area. (2) Should the committee compile and publish publications for publicity purposes? (Resolution) 1. The committee's business report should be published within a limited time. Materials should be provided by the committee members as much as possible. 2. Compile a booklet in plain language on the organization methods and cooperative significance of cooperative societies for publicity purposes. (3) If the Bureau of Social Affairs approves the recruitment of workers' consumer cooperation instructors, how should the committee assist in the handling? (Resolution) First, request the Bureau of Social Affairs to publish recruitment advertisements, conduct screening, and then organize an examination committee to hold a re-examination.

Three provinces suffered, and our Changyuan was particularly severe. Fortunately, we received your thoughtful and generous aid, charitable broth, and righteous garments, which were well distributed. We have received the virtue of life and the kindness of clothing and bedding. Our gratitude cannot be expressed in words. Unexpectedly, as the hope for life was just beginning to turn, a sudden flood occurred. Within a day and night, more than a hundred villages along both banks of the dike were again submerged. The old, the young, women, and children climbed onto roofs and trees, and their cries were extremely miserable. Boats were used to rescue them, but ice piled up, and the currents rushed wildly. The disaster victims who did not die from drowning were certainly frozen to death by the ice. But no matter what, how can we bear to sit idly by and see them all perish? We rely even more on boats to cross the waters. Now, the staff of the National Government's investigation and release office and various charitable organizations have joined our association to send personnel to rush to the scene and rescue them in various ways, while also distributing steamed food and setting up shelters in the city to accommodate them, preparing porridge kitchens, and arranging them separately to relieve them from the pain of drowning and to avoid the suffering of displacement. However, the vast area of hundreds of miles and the countless households mean that spring is approaching, and I fear that a drop in the bucket will not be able to remedy the situation. We implore all kind-hearted people to act with compassion and benevolence and quickly continue to issue large sums of money so that this continuous grant can save these suffering people. Life and death, flesh and bones, is what we hope for. The survivors of the disaster are anxious and cannot choose their words. We urgently send this appeal to the compassionate. We humbly beg your kind consideration and respectfully wish you peace and prosperity."

The Number of Poor People at the Zhabei Porridge Kitchen is Increasing Daily 164

More than 30 loads of rice for porridge

More than 10,000 people eat porridge

The Zhabei Charity Group Porridge Kitchen, located at the Third Porridge Kitchen on Liuying Road, opened on January 15th. Every day from 6:00 AM to 9:00 AM, the elderly, weak, women, and children in the area went to the kitchen to eat porridge. In the beginning, there were only a few thousand people, but the number increased daily, and now there are more than 10,000 people. Eight porridge stoves have been opened, and the amount of rice for porridge has increased to more than 30 loads. The kitchen is spacious and can accommodate many people. As winter passes and spring arrives, the weather is uncertain with rain and snow. Reed sheds have already been built with 250 units, and bamboo benches are placed inside for the women and children to rest after receiving porridge. In addition to hearing that directors Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, and Jin Tingsun have each donated rice, it was recently heard that Director Lin Kanghou has raised 1,500 yuan in donations. Director Wang Binyan of the group is concerned that with so many people and so much porridge, the funds are extremely exhausted and may be difficult to maintain.

Xing Zhigang Asks to Investigate Forced Donations to Ships 165

Xing Zhigang, the representative of the shipowners in Pudong, submitted a document to the Municipal Government yesterday, stating: "Presenting for falsely claiming a name, illegally forcing donations, urging the Social Affairs Bureau, Public Security Bureau, and Public Works Bureau to strictly investigate and uphold municipal affairs. Recently, it has been reported that the various shipowners at the South Assembly Hall, Dongjiadu, and Gongyi Wharf have reported that there are groups of three to five people loitering around the various harbors, holding leaflets, receipt books, and a bundle of small lead tags, forcibly collecting fees for tagging each ship at one yuan, arbitrarily coercing them. The ignorant shipowners, not knowing the truth, have been deceived. Upon inspection, the leaflets are in the name of the Shipping and Lighterage Industry Workers' United Benefit Association, stating that there are approximately 60,000 to 70,000 ships traveling to various places in the city, and in order to seek long-term benefits, they must quickly join the association, etc. The leaflets list as many as five offices, so the extent of their extortion can be imagined. It has been verified that the establishment of associations and gatherings is freely participated in by the same industry, and there is no reason for compulsory membership. Moreover, the name of the Workers' United Benefit Association violates the Public Association Law, and there is no compulsory fee for tagging. Moreover, the rural ships are ships for the convenience of the people, and their nature is completely different from that of the lighterage industry. How can they be forced to join? It is obviously intimidating the ignorant rural people, forcing donations under a false name, and harming the citizens, which is not trivial. Therefore, I am submitting the leaflets and receipts to your office, respectfully requesting your examination and approval, and immediately instructing the Social Affairs Bureau, Public Security Bureau, and Public Works Bureau to investigate the truth thoroughly and strictly and to benefit the shipping industry and uphold municipal affairs. It would be a great service."

Editor-in-Chief of Shanghai Business News Sentenced to Imprisonment for Publishing News About the Xu Case 168

Newspaper Association held a meeting to discuss yesterday

Reporters Association scheduled to hold a meeting today

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Shanghai Business News was founded in October of the year before last. Manager Sun Mingqi and Editor-in-Chief Zhang Jiping. In addition to publishing domestic and foreign news on politics, military affairs, society, etc., the content also focuses on commercial news. It is recognized as the official gazette by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations. Since its publication, it has been developing daily. However, recently, the newspaper was suddenly sued by Ji Juemi for publishing news about the Xu Yuying case, and Editor-in-Chief Zhang Jiping was sentenced to imprisonment in the Special District Local Court, which caused a major reaction in the journalism community. The details of this matter are explored and recorded as follows:

Details of the Case 169

A young woman named Xu Yuying previously sued Ji Juemi, the chief steward of the Hardoon Garden, in the First Special District Local Court for the crime of seduction. At the beginning of the case, the Shanghai Business News received a contribution from outside and sent an outside reporter to investigate. It was confirmed that there was a lawsuit. Therefore, on December 4th of last year, the newspaper published the news truthfully without adding or subtracting anything. The next day, the newspaper received a letter from Ye Fokang representing Ji Juemi, strongly arguing that it was a fabrication. The newspaper published the original letter on the 7th. However, the original letter contained words such as "will definitely be prosecuted." The newspaper also added a brief reply. Ji Juemi then hired lawyer Xue Dubi and filed a defamation lawsuit against Sun Mingqi, the manager of the newspaper, and Zhang Jiping, the editor-in-chief, for damaging his reputation. At the same time, Sun Mingqi, who was not responsible for the editing, also hired lawyer Jiang Chiping and filed a counterclaim against Ji Juemi for false accusation because the main body of Ji Juemi's accusation was wrong.

Sentenced to Imprisonment 170

The case was tried several times by Deng Baosun, the judge of the First Special District Local Court. Zhang Jiping also hired lawyer Jiang Chiping to defend him, stating that he published the information based on the submissions and did not add or subtract anything. He had never met Ji Juemi before and had no intention to do so. Therefore, he was not criminally liable under the law. The debate was declared closed at around 4:00 PM on the 25th of last month. The verdict was announced at 9:00 AM the next morning. Sun Mingqi was found not guilty. Ji Juemi was found not guilty on the counterclaim. Zhang Jiping was sentenced to four months of imprisonment, and the judgment was to be published in the Shen Bao and the Xin Bao.

Two Associations Express Support 171

After hearing the verdict, the newspaper considered it to be obviously biased and feared that if such a precedent were set, the future of the journalism industry would be unimaginable. Therefore, in addition to filing an appeal to seek legal relief, it has also reported the situation to the Newspaper Association and the Reporters Association, requesting them to uphold justice. After receiving the report, the Newspaper Association convened a meeting for discussion yesterday afternoon, and the Reporters Association is also scheduled to hold a meeting for discussion this afternoon. The newspaper issued a notice to all sectors yesterday, stating:

Guan Yuting and His Wife Save on Food and Clothing to Help Disaster Relief 172

Yesterday, it was heard that Mr. Guan Yuting and his wife personally sent 1,000 yuan, which they saved on food and clothing, to the Society's office and requested that it be immediately remitted to the disaster area to save the disaster victims. The Murderer Who Shot Li Min Zhou Confessed Eloquently in Court 182

Zhou Zhan Yuan Directly Admitted to the Assassination of Li

Li's Body Was Taken to the International Funeral Parlor

Li Min Zhou, the Cantonese general manager of the New New Company on Nanjing Road, was shot in the abdomen by Zhou Zhan Yuan, a Dalian man who had been dismissed from his position as the general superintendent of the company, at 5 p.m. the day before yesterday. He died immediately. The murderer was also arrested. The details have already been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Detective Liu Xiang Zhai of the General Police Department, together with a foreign detective, escorted Zhou to the First Special District Court. Judge Feng Shi De presided over the trial. Lawyer Li Zhi Shan of the Police Department first stated the circumstances of the tragic case, saying that Zhou Zhan Yuan followed Li Min Zhou from the New New Company to room 327 of the New New Hotel. After shooting Li with a handgun, Li was wounded and exited the room, entering room 305, where he collapsed and died. The murderer then fled with the weapon, fleeing directly to the Guohua Bank on Beijing Road, intending to borrow travel expenses from the doorman No. 2139 of the bank to escape to Fengtian. At that time, the doorman had not yet started his shift, so the murderer waited until 8 p.m., when the doorman arrived, and then told him about the incident. Because the murderer was still wearing the New New uniform, the doorman ordered him to go to the eighth floor of the Guohua Building to change clothes. The doorman then reported to the General Police Department. The central and western detectives were immediately dispatched to arrest him. A handgun was found in his pocket. However, it was observed that there was a bullet stuck in the barrel, which has not yet been removed, so it cannot be presented as evidence to avoid danger. However, this murderer is so cruel, and should be tried in accordance with Article 264, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. Then Detective Liu reported the circumstances of the arrest of the defendant. Zhou Zhan Yuan confessed that when Liu Xi Ji, the former general manager of New New, worked at Sincere Company, he was hired by Liu and had served for seven years. Later, Liu left Sincere and founded New New, and he also followed Liu to the New New preparation office, and borrowed 500 yuan to purchase one share of New New stock. It has been eight years, and the dividends received have far exceeded the interest on the debt, so the stock has already been mortgaged. His family's livelihood depends entirely on the 28 yuan monthly salary he earns as the general superintendent of New New. However, at 5 p.m. yesterday, General Manager Zhou summoned him to his office and suddenly ordered him to hand over the keys to all the doors under his management and dismissed him. He was terrified and asked him to announce his mistakes. He said that because he was old and weak, he replied that if he was too old to be the general superintendent, he asked him to change him to another job to avoid unemployment. But Li refused and turned to leave the room. He also followed out to the room, then he knelt on the ground to beg, Li still refused, and went to the New New Hotel. He went there again. When they arrived in room 327, Li was undressing and was about to take a bath. He then knelt down for the third time, and when Li saw this, he suddenly turned his body around. At this time, he was filled with anger and did not have time to consider the consequences. He reached into the pocket of his uniform and pulled out the handgun and fired a shot, whether it hit him or not, he did not.

New Seedling Planting Techniques Discovered in the North and South Markets of Shanghai 189

Falsely Claiming Household Registration Donation and Collecting Two Horns Per Household

The Third Office of the First District Has Issued a Notice to Pay Attention to Residents

Recently, young men with fanciful ideas, wearing luxurious clothes, carrying black leather bags, and resembling civil servants, have been collecting household registration donations from shops and residents in the Nanshi and Zhabei areas, at two horns per household, and issuing receipts printed with the words "Household Registration Office of the Police Department of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau" and stamped with a picture stamp with the words "Two Horns in Silver Dollars". They claimed to be employees of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. This household registration donation was recently created by the Municipal Public Security Bureau and approved by the Municipal Government, and stipulates that all households, regardless of size, residing in this city must pay this donation of two horns in silver dollars. If they dare to resist and refuse to pay, they will be severely punished by the Bureau. Therefore, the shops and residents did not investigate deeply because the amount was small and paid the money as required, so that in a few days, thousands of shops and residents in the north and south markets were defrauded. It was not until yesterday morning that the matter was heard by Jin Dianyang, the director of the Third Office of the First District, who stated that the Municipal Public Security Bureau had not created this household registration donation and sent personnel to collect it. It was clear that the young men were inventing names and defrauding people of money, which was extremely illegal. Therefore, in addition to ordering his subordinates to investigate, he also issued a notice as follows: Notice to all residents, it has been found that unscrupulous people have recently falsely claimed the name of the Household Registration Office of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and have been collecting festival fees from door to door, collecting two horns in silver dollars per household. These unscrupulous people dare to defraud people of money, which is extremely illegal. In addition to this office strictly investigating and severely punishing them, all residents should be aware of this and not be deceived. If you encounter the above situation, immediately hand them over to the nearby police post and take them to the office for strict handling.

Director of the Jiaxing Grain Collection Office

Embezzled More Than 40,000 Yuan in Public Funds

Gao Yuchun, a native of Jiaxing, was the director of the Grain Collection Office of the Jiaxing Finance Bureau. He was suspected of embezzling more than 40,000 yuan in public funds and abandoning his post to flee. The director of the bureau found out and asked the local authorities to pay attention to the investigation. Director Wang learned that Gao was hiding at No. 58, Lane 351, Hart Road, Shanghai, and sent a letter to the county government to transfer the case to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and request the First Special District Court to issue an arrest warrant. At 6:30 a.m. the day before yesterday, the Jing'an Temple Police Station was ordered to send Chinese and Western detectives, together with Gu Liancheng and Hu Guisheng, detectives from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, to secretly arrest him at the address. However, Gao Yuchun had already heard the news and fled. Only his son, Gao Anke, lived in the house. The police station, based on the report of the detectives of the Public Security Bureau, said that Gao Anke was also involved, so they asked the First Special Court to issue an arrest warrant for Gao Anke, arrested Gao, and took him to the police station for detention. Then Wu Jinsheng, an employee of the Jiaxing Finance Bureau, reported that the defendant's father, Gao Yuchun, had embezzled more than 40,000 yuan in public funds and fled, so he was ordered to be investigated. Since Gao Yuchun had already heard the news and fled far away, his son Gao Anke was arrested, because his father had embezzled state public funds, his son should be held responsible, etc. When Gao Anke was questioned, he confessed that he had been working in the advertising business in the newspaper office and had been in Shanghai for 13 years. He did not know where his father, Gao Yuchun, currently lived. His mother and others were all in the countryside in Jiaxing, and he knew nothing about what his father had done. Judge Xue Zhonghe reviewed the confession and ordered Gao Anke to be released on bail pending trial.

Yuan Zhiyuan Died on the Spot

Worldwide Chess Master's Shanghai Anniversary Celebration 194

The entire staff of the Shanghai International Chess Club held a celebration last night in the dining room on the third floor of the YMCA to commemorate the anniversary of the worldwide chess master, Dr. Emanuel Lasker, coming to Shanghai to play chess. All the lights in the room were turned off, red candles were lit, and the room was filled with fresh flowers, as well as portraits of Lasker and various international chess silver shields. Russia's Bogoljubov, Czechoslovakia, Finland, etc. won a total of three games. China's Pan Jishi, Yang Wenkai, etc. won a total of four games. The second time, without using a timer, in a round robin of twelve games, Russia's Cui Yi, etc. won a total of two games, and China's Xie Xiasun, America's Eli, etc. won a total of six games. All of these results have been published on the largest silver shield. Commemorative medals and chess scores, etc. were given to all the champions, runners-up, and those who won or drew for the first time in this session, which were distributed on the spot by Mr. Danay's daughter. Because of political relations, Lasker had already left Russian nationality and joined French nationality. After signing, everyone gathered in the hall to the right of the YMCA to hold a rapid chess competition, in which each move could not exceed one minute at the latest.

Expert Dr. Xue Si Hai in Charge

The Shanghai Tuberculosis Sanatorium at No. 4 West Avenue in this city has been working hard to implement tuberculosis prevention for many years. The second is a shockproof X-ray machine with a TutoValve device, which is the latest X-ray machine equipment in the world. The hospital has now first prepared it and it is on the way to Shanghai. The Splendor of Labor Publications in the 23rd Year 197

"International Labour" is a monthly publication recently compiled and printed by the China Branch of the International Labour Office. The purpose of its publication is to introduce domestic and foreign labor treatises, news, and the work of the International Labour Organization. Because the publication has specialized characteristics, the selected treatises, news, special reports, etc. are all rare materials. The inaugural issue of "International Labour" has been published at the end of January. Its main content includes Li Pingheng's "Prerequisites for the Implementation of Factory Inspection in China," Deng Yuzhi's "A Brief Record of a Visit to a Contract Labor Workshop," Guo Zidong's "Prospects for International Labour in 1934," and other treatises. In addition, there are domestic and foreign labor news and the draft conventions passed by the 17th International Labour Conference, totaling no less than 100,000 words. It is indeed a rare publication. The retail price is 20 cents per copy, and the annual subscription for twelve issues is two dollars, with no additional postage within China. The sales outlets in Shanghai are the Modern, Guanghua, Liming, and Nanjing bookstores, and the China Branch of the International Labour Office on the second floor of No. 868 Jing'an Temple Road.

Gratitude Turns to Enmity, Adultery with a Friend's Wife, Shameless Man and Woman Still Seek Appeal 199

The Facts of the Case Are Clear, How Can They Rely on Sophistry

The Court Sentences Each to Ten Months Imprisonment

Yang Junhao, also known as Wensheng, a 29-year-old man from Tangqiao, Pudong, originally worked in the pawnshop business. In the spring and summer of the year before last, because he was unemployed and destitute, he was taken in by his friend Zhang Guilin, a local resident of No. 18 Yongyu Lane, Beile Road, French Concession. Unexpectedly, Yang became lustful and repaid kindness with hatred. In June of that year, while Zhang was in Beijing seeking a job, he seduced Zhang's wife, Qin, into adultery. After Zhang returned home, his eldest daughter, Jinfeng, told him what had happened, and Zhang drove Yang out, forbidding him from entering his house and severing contact. However, Yang secretly instigated Qin to run away and live with him at No. 72 Ronghua Lane, Malan Road, living together like husband and wife. Zhang found out and reported to the patrol, which sent detectives to arrest them. Yang happened to be out, so only Qin was arrested. Qin confessed her guilt to her husband, begged for forgiveness, and vowed not to associate with Yang again, begging to be spared from investigation. Zhang, seeing that his wife had realized her mistake, agreed and asked the patrol chief to spare her from further investigation. After taking her back, Qin and Yang's adulterous affair continued passionately, and soon she often brought her five-year-old daughter, Jinxia, to Yang's small room in the pavilion at No. 687 Malan Road for adulterous trysts, and ordered the girl to call Yang "Daddy." Later, the girl told her father, and Zhang called the 350th patrol and rushed to catch them in the act, dragging Qin and Yang out of bed and taking them to the patrol, who sent them to the Second Special District Court for prosecution. The interrogation and investigation details have been recorded in previous reports. Yesterday, Judge Qiu continued the interrogation in Criminal Court No. 8. The patrol lawyer Chen Ming explained the case and the investigation process. When questioned, Qin confessed that she had gone to Yang to borrow money and was arrested by her husband, and denied that she had committed adultery. Yang also flatly denied it. After reviewing the statements in court, because the case had been proven, there was no room for sophistry. The court sentenced Zhang Qin and Yang Junhao to ten months imprisonment each. The two defendants stated that they were not satisfied with the verdict and requested an appeal. The court granted the request and ordered them to be held in custody pending further instructions.

After the factory notified the deceased's sister, Ms. Jin Guangmei, she arrived at the scene and believed that her brother's death was unclear. She filed a petition with the local court requesting an autopsy. It is now known that this case was entrusted to Prosecutor Li Fen, who, together with Examiner Xuan Zhiming and others, crossed the river to the factory for an autopsy. According to Dr. Li Shijiu of the factory, the deceased, Jin Guangdou, had heart failure and his body temperature was 39 degrees. Although he was given an emergency injection, it was still impossible to save him. After Prosecutor Li and others examined the body, they determined that he had died of illness and filled out the form, ordering the family to collect the body and await instructions.

De Tai Secondhand Store Careless 205

The De Tai Secondhand Store on Hejian Road, Yangtai Pu Lan Road, caught fire carelessly at 0:45 yesterday noon. The flames immediately broke through the roof, burning down two bungalows, and a large number of clothes and packages stored inside, worth more than 10,000 yuan, were all burned to ashes. Gambling Syndicate Not Satisfied with Sentence 206

Wang Youlan Sentenced to Eight Months Imprisonment

Shanghai is a place where people from all walks of life gather, both good and bad, and gambling scams are often heard of. Even in the Nanshi area, a gambling scam has recently resulted in a murder. It was found that in the Nanyang Inn outside Xiaodongmen, Zhang Guochu, a pig merchant, was cheated out of 360 yuan by the famous gambling syndicate Wang Youlan, also known as Wang Shaocheng, in collusion with accomplices, who opened a room in the inn and set up a gambling game. Wang forced Zhang to write an IOU, and Zhang jumped out of the window in desperation and died (as reported in this newspaper). It is now known that the French Patrol arrested Wang Shaocheng, that is, Youlan, and brought him to the Second Special District Local Court. Yesterday afternoon, the court opened a hearing. After the plaintiff stated the circumstances of Zhang Guochu's forced suicide, Wang Shaocheng was brought to court for a debate. The court sentenced Wang Shaocheng to eight months of imprisonment and fined him 200 yuan. For the private prosecution, Wang Shaocheng was ordered to compensate the deceased's family 360 yuan. After the verdict, Wang Shaocheng stated that he was not satisfied and was allowed to file an appeal during the appeal period, stating the reasons for his dissatisfaction.

Streetcar Runs Over Girl, Severing Both Legs and Causing Death 207

Wu Xiangbao, a Ningbo native residing at No. 3 Siping Lane, Yingdong Road, Xiaoximen East, had a seven-year-old daughter, Aifen, who was taken to the Deji Barber Shop on Zhonghua Road by her aunt Xu Yuyan for a haircut at about 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. She was hit by a South China streetcar, severing both legs. She was immediately sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. Liu Huaiqing, the driver who caused the accident, was arrested by the police and detained at the Second Division of the Second District. It is now known that Wu Aifen died of her injuries in the hospital in the evening due to the severity of her injuries and could not be saved. Yesterday morning, Qin Defang, the local head of the 27th Patrol, reported the case to the local court for an autopsy. He was then entrusted to Prosecutor Ouyang to examine the body at the hospital and ordered the family to collect the body and await the police's handling of the driver who caused the accident.

According to the Japanese "Mainichi Shimbun" yesterday, the northern branch of the Shanghai Japanese Residents' Road Federation held an extraordinary general meeting at the Kabuki-za at 3:00 PM on the 28th of last month to discuss the rent reduction movement. Japanese Merchant Violates Drug Sales Regulations, Lightly Fined and Released 212

According to the Japanese "Shanghai Daily" yesterday, Tetsuzo Yanagida, a Japanese merchant residing at No. 384 Wusong Road, secretly sold aphrodisiacs to Chinese without permission. This was discovered by the Hongkou Public Works Department. The suspect and the drugs were sent to the Consulate-General. It was found that he often carried drugs similar to morphine and heroin to Chinese pharmacies for sale. After inspection, it was found that they were energy-boosting agents produced by the Ikeda Taikaren Pharmaceutical Company, sold for 100 yuan per pound. However, he did not obtain permission from the police and sold them without authorization, violating the drug sales regulations. The Japanese Consulate-General has fined him 10 yuan and released him.

Bingxun Shorthand Primer Published 213

The Bingxun Shorthand School on Gaoshou Lane, Hainin Road, Shanghai, has recently printed a Bingxun Shorthand Primer, which was published today. It is simple and easy to learn, and can be learned without a teacher. Those who are illiterate can learn to read, write, and read newspapers after learning it. Those who are literate can write faster after reading it, which is a great contribution to Chinese culture. The book was written by Mr. Yang in memory of his uncle, Yang Chiqing. It costs only 40 cents per copy. Mr. Yang lost his education at a young age and was fortunate to have the opportunity to study thanks to his uncle's savings. It is reported that libraries and mass education centers in various places have enthusiastically ordered the Bingxun Shorthand Primer.

Board Meeting of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture

(Nanjing, 2nd) The Board of Directors of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture held its eighth regular meeting at the Academia Sinica on the morning of the 2nd. Board members Hu Shih, Li Shizeng, Ren Hongjun, Zhou Yichun, Jin Zhiji, Xu Xinliu, Baker Bernode, Stuart Lei Deng, and representatives from the Ministry of Education Chen Shizhen, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Liu Shishun, totaling over ten people, were present. The meeting adjourned at 12:45. The Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center of this City is Soliciting Contributions for Compiling Party Ideology Series

Notification to All Schools from the Municipal Bureau of Education

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education yesterday issued an order to all levels of schools in the city, stating: "Regarding the letter from the Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center, which states that, to promote the Three People's Principles and enrich the teaching materials on Party ideology, a series of fifty books on Party ideology will be compiled and completed in two years. The rules for soliciting contributions and the first batch of book titles are enclosed. Please forward this information to all levels of schools under your jurisdiction for notification, which will be for public convenience, etc." In addition to replying to the letter, these rules for soliciting contributions are hereby copied and sent to all schools for notification. This order is issued.

Attached are the Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center's rules for soliciting contributions for compiling the Party Ideology Series and the first batch of book titles: (1) Eligibility for Submission: Limited to current civic education teachers and instructors in various schools. (2) Submission Procedures: Before the end of February in the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the submitter should first register with the Center, providing detailed information on their name, age, native place, gender, educational background, name and position of their current school, date and number of their Party membership card, date and number of their Party ideology teacher certification, the book title they wish to compile, the editing purpose and outline, and a list of references. After the Party Ideology Series Review Committee of the Center approves the submitter's editing purpose and outline, a formal commission letter will be sent. Those who fail the review will be notified separately by letter. (3) Word Count: Each book should be between 20,000 and 50,000 words. (4) Style: Primarily in vernacular Chinese. (5) Payment: Five silver dollars per thousand words. (6) Book Titles: A Brief History of Revolutions in Various Countries, The National Revolution, Nation and State, Colonies and Semi-Colonies, A General Overview of the Powers' Aggression Against China, The Five-Power Constitution, A Brief History of the Civil Rights Movement in Various Countries, Democratic Politics, Tutelage and Constitutionalism, The Principle of People's Livelihood vs. Communism, The Principle of People's Livelihood vs. Socialism, The Principle of People's Livelihood vs. Capitalism, Labor-Management Cooperation, Cooperative Movements in Various Countries, Psychological Reconstruction, Industrial Plan, Regulation of Capital, Equalization of Land Ownership, A General Overview of Chinese Agriculture, The State of Chinese Industry, Chinese Disaster Relief and Rural Programs, The Chinese Grain Problem, The Silk and Cotton Industries, Government of the People, by the People, for the People.

Principal Wang Suben of the Private Minli Girls' High School Resigns Due to Accepting Responsibility

The Board of Directors Has Already Been Automatically Reorganized

A New Principal Will Be Elected at Today's Meeting

The Private Minli Girls' High School in this city, since Secretary Wang Dazao organized a drama club and propagated communism, leading to his arrest by the Garrison Headquarters, Principal Wang Suben has resigned due to accepting responsibility. The Board of Directors has also been automatically reorganized. Details are as follows:

The Principal Has Resigned

Wang Suben has served as the principal of the school since its founding over twenty years ago. He has been able to manage school affairs adequately. In recent years, due to age and declining strength, he has repeatedly expressed his intention to resign to the Board of Directors, but it was not approved. Several days ago, after the school's secretary, Wang Dazao, was arrested by the Garrison Headquarters for propagating communism at the request of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Principal Wang took responsibility for his oversight and expressed his retirement. He has formally submitted his resignation to the Board of Directors, which was promptly approved. However, in recognition of his years of service in education, a reward will be considered as a form of commemoration.

Reorganization of the Board of Directors

Since Wang Dazao's arrest, the Municipal Bureau of Education, following a letter from the Municipal Party Headquarters, ordered the school's Board of Directors to reorganize itself to bring about a fresh start. It was decided to automatically reorganize. A meeting of the Board of Directors was held at the East Asia Restaurant the other day, where it was decided to comply with the order to reorganize. Tong Xingbai, Liu Yazi, Wang Yansong, Wu Xingya, Qian Xinzhi, Yang Weiyu, Huang Xianggu, Zhu Xuefan, Cai Hongtian, Tang Subennan, Wang Yiting, Zhu Yinong, Zhu Xiangwan, Chen Jicheng, and Su Yingjie were elected as the fifteen new directors. It is reported that the Chairman of the Board of Directors, Ye Hongying, has already submitted a report on the automatic reorganization to the Municipal Bureau of Education, stating that Principal Wang Suben has resigned and that a new principal will be elected soon. The Municipal Bureau of Education immediately approved the report and ordered the convening of the first meeting of the reorganized Board of Directors to elect a principal to take over and reorganize the school, and to issue appointment letters. The first meeting of the reorganized Board of Directors will be held at the school on Xiaoximen today (the 3rd) at 5:00 PM.

Record of the Jiaotong University's Northern Expedition (2)

| A 1-1 Tie with Qinghua in the Second Match in Beiping |

A 0-0 Tie with Beining Yesterday in Tianjin

Match with the Tianjin Chinese Team Tomorrow

(Tianjin, 1st) The Shanghai Jiaotong University soccer team, consisting of sixteen people, arrived in Tianjin from Beiping on the 1st. The Beining Sports Association hosted a banquet. The team played against the Beining team at the Beining Stadium on the 2nd and will play against the Chinese team on the 3rd. The order of matches for the remaining teams has not been determined.

Tianjin, 2nd Special Dispatch: The Shanghai Jiaotong University soccer team played against the Beining team at the Beining Stadium at 3:30 PM on the 2nd. There were a thousand spectators. The competition was fierce in both halves, and the result was a tie. The Fuda soccer team has arrived in Tianjin and is scheduled to play against the Tianjin mixed team at the soccer field at 3:00 PM on the 3rd. The mixed team of Fuda and the Tianjin soccer team will be the representative team attending the Shanghai-Hong Kong-Tianjin tournament. The Jiaotong University vs. Tianjin Chinese team soccer match is scheduled for 4:30 PM on the 4th at the Nankai Stadium.

Heading to the Tsinghua Garden

The Shanghai Jiaotong University soccer team went on a northern expedition to Beiping. In the first match against Furen, they unfortunately lost. On the 30th, they met the Tsinghua University soccer team. The time was 2:30 PM, and the location was Tsinghua Garden. The referee was still Wang Zhensheng. The Tsinghua team has many veterans from the North China soccer world, including goalkeeper Zhao Yansheng, defender Xiao Difei, and center forward Huang Zhongfu, all of whom are famous players. Although the Jiaotong University team unfortunately lost to Furen in the first match, they were even more careful in this match.

The Big Battle Begins

After the kickoff, the Jiaotong University team immediately launched an attack with short passes, with a fierce momentum. The Tsinghua players were not without resistance, and they bravely fought back. The small ball changed direction and was fiercely shot towards the Jiaotong University goal. Fortunately, goalkeeper Fan Jiaju was quick on his feet and saved the goal. Afterwards, both sides had excellent performances.

Jiaotong University Takes the Lead

Jiaotong University forward Wan Xianghua received a pass but was kicked out of bounds by Xiao Difei. The Tsinghua defense was on the verge of collapse. Amidst the stampede, the Tsinghua defender was penalized with a twelve-yard penalty kick. With a flick of Ji Guangzhong's foot, Zhao Yansheng, despite his experience, was helpless. After the kickoff again, there was a lot of contention, but there were no results. In the first half, Jiaotong University took the lead with a score of 1-0.

Tsinghua's Last-Ditch Effort

At the start of the second half, Tsinghua changed their offensive strategy after being instructed by Old Man Ma, using the left side to advance. Xiong Dazhen had great ambition and intended to take revenge. Receiving a supply from the rear, he immediately spurred his horse and galloped towards the Jiaotong University base camp. Old Cow Huang Zhongfu saw an opportunity and charged forward from the center.

1-1 Draw

Xiong Dazhen passed the ball and shot hard, and the ball responded as desired, much to the delight of the surrounding spectators, who felt even better than taking a soothing pill. Time was unforgiving, and the battle time had arrived in an instant. The result was 1-1, with both sides drawing. The lineups of the two armies are on the left:

French Business Association's Two Failures Make It Difficult to Secure the Group A Championship

The French Business Association, which had nine wins in nine matches in the first cycle of the West Football Association's Group A, has recently suffered consecutive defeats. First, they lost 1-2 to West Capture, and then they lost 2-4 to Huacesi, indirectly giving Donghua a chance to win the championship. Donghua currently has one draw and three losses, and Donghua's meeting with the French Business Association today is a very good opportunity to "recover." If Donghua can defeat the French Business Association again, making the French Business Association also lose three times, they will only have one more point than Donghua. If another team can defeat the French Business Association again, Donghua can compete for the throne. West Capture has three draws and two losses, and Youyou has one draw and three losses, so they are all in the same position. Therefore, if Donghua wins against the French Business Association, they will also indirectly give West Capture and Youyou a chance to compete for the championship. However, if things proceed according to this ideal, Donghua will have the highest chance of winning the championship.

The Absence of Donghua's Generals Increases Hope and Then Reduces It Again

However, the weather is unpredictable, and fortune and misfortune are uncertain. It is a pity that Donghua cannot take advantage of this only opportunity at this critical moment. It is well known that Li Ning and Wan Xianghua are the souls of Donghua's front and back lines. Now that they cannot play and there are no substantial substitutes, the reporter specifically asked the team manager last night who would replace them. According to reports, they have not yet found suitable talent and must make a decision at the last minute. The sigh of difficult talent is precarious, and the opportunity created by others will be given away again.
