Business News, Finance

The issue of settlement price changes for spot gold, delayed the market opening

Continued to rise by six dollars and ninety cents after twists and turns

Recently, the United States has reduced the gold content in its currency and changed the value of the US dollar to 5906. The US President has announced that this will be implemented on February 1st, hence changes should be made to spot gold settlement prices. This will be handled according to Article 47 of the Gold Exchange's operating rules. However, brokers believe that the exchange's announcement was too late, only being released after the market closed on February 1st. As such, many in the industry were unaware, resulting in unsettled transactions. Moreover, short sellers believed the settlement price change was unfavorable to them, leading to queries with the exchange authorities. As there were no results at the time, no one was willing to trade, resulting in a market uproar. After an emergency meeting and debate between the exchange authorities and the brokers' association, an understanding was reached, and the market reopened as usual in the afternoon. The exchange's announcement is recorded below: Reuters telegrams from various parties this month confirm that the United States has announced a reduction in the weight of the existing currency system. All spot gold transactions for February and March that have already been concluded should be handled in accordance with the exchange's operating rules, using the initial HSBC exchange rate quoted on January 31st of last month as the standard. It was found that HSBC quoted one shilling four pence one two five on that day, and the US exchange rate was thirty-three yuan and fifty cents, equivalent to an Anglo-American exchange rate of 498605. For the end of February and the end of March, the initial HSBC exchange rate will be used, calculated at 498605, with the US exchange rate still calculated at two hundred and forty yuan, equivalent to one tael of spot gold. Before the end of the expiration date, trading will continue as usual. Besides notifying the brokers' association, this is a special announcement. Furthermore, no swaps will be held in March in order to clear the settlement price. However, a decision will be made after another meeting in April. The market situation yesterday afternoon started strong but then softened, with many twists and turns. The will of the traders was hesitant, so prices fluctuated greatly. This unexpected change in events. The highest price was 713 yuan and 80 cents, and the lowest was 706 yuan and 60 cents, a difference of 7 yuan and 20 cents. Most of the long and short positions were squared off, and the market ended up rising 6 yuan and 90 cents. The market opened up 9 yuan and 90 cents from opening, totaling 711 yuan and 70 cents. The spot and forward silver markets both fell, and the exchange rates for British pounds and US dollars both dropped by half a cent and five cents respectively, which stimulated the Shanghai market. Trading began before the market opened, with initial quotes of sixteen to seventeen yuan. The Dalian gang, Wanxing, first bought more than one hundred taels, and then, due to the unloading of Hengyu, Dachangxiang, Hengtai, and sporadic long positions, the price plummeted by more than ten yuan, reaching the level of 06 yuan. It then rose again to more than 12 yuan when the market opened. Goods opened at 11 yuan and 30 cents. After opening, Hengxing, Dafa, Yongyifeng, Yongda, the Dalian gang, etc. all went in, and as the exchange rate for drafts continued to strengthen, Mitsui absorbed 6875 for June US dollars, and then added up to 13 yuan and 80 cents. Unexpectedly, Hengyu, Xie Xing, Yong, etc. came to sell, and the price immediately depreciated to 09 yuan. Bingxing and Shenkang came in, adding slightly more than one yuan, totaling 10 yuan and 30 cents. After 2:20 PM, the exchange rate for drafts loosened, and major players on the floor dumped. It is estimated that Dachangxiang, Hengxing, Yuan Zhifeng, Yong, and a certain speculator sold a large amount. By 3:00 PM, the May US dollar could be settled at 8125, and then at 3:30 PM it was 06 yuan and 60 cents. Afterwards, Hengyu, Zhifeng, Yong, and Fuyu all went in again. At 4:00 PM, it was 09 yuan and 70 cents, and then fluctuated around 09 yuan. When the market closed at 4:30 PM, it was 08 yuan and 70 cents (goods were auctioned at 8 yuan and 60 cents). Afterward, trading continued in the 9 yuan range. Hengyu and Wanxing bought in, while Dachangxiang continued to sell. Spot gold was at 1,130 yuan, with limited trading. Decorative gold increased by another 2 yuan, totaling 116 yuan.

Quoted prices are now based on the Anglo-American exchange rate calculated at 498605. Yesterday, the British gold rate was one shilling and four pence (plus two pence), using one shilling and six pence as a multiplier, and then using 240 as a divisor, which is equivalent to 33 yuan and 25 US dollars, approximately 722 yuan. Initially, there was a premium of around 10 yuan, and then around 14 yuan, which was about 3 yuan less than the previous day. The registration fee was 23 yuan for February and 09 yuan for March, with a water supplement of 23 yuan.

Floor transactions varied. Short covering was very strong. According to statistics, Bingxing, Dafa Yong, Shenkang, Yuan Maoyong, Ruikang, Yuanchun, Sida, Yuanxing Yong, and Shunli all went in. Dachangxiang sold more than 2,000 taels (sold off), Zhifeng Yong, Yifeng Yong, Futai Heng, Hengtai, Hengxing Yuan, and a Mr. Lu all sold. It was heard that a Mr. Wu sold a huge amount through a certain firm. Fuyu and Hengyu went out and then in again. The rest was complicated, but not in large quantities. The Dalian gang bought and sold more than 2,000 taels in total. There were still exchange rate hedges. The Guang Gang Hengxing slightly entered 2-300 taels. The quota of each firm in March was reduced by another 3,800 taels, totaling 35,427 taels.

Various Securities Firms Seemed to Have Contracted

The Bond Market Circulated and Tended to Be Stagnant

Yesterday, the market of the Chinese Securities Exchange turned from circulating to stagnant. Major players did not enter or exit the market at all, and trading suddenly felt idle. Because the Lunar New Year was approaching, new transactions were extremely rare. Besides a few settlements and swaps that slightly entered and exited the market, speculators were temporarily dormant, and those with slightly thicker capital were waiting and watching for changes, thus forming a stalemate. It was heard that the market would be closed starting next Saturday, with about nine days of holiday including the week. Therefore, those who were floating long or short positions would have to swap or settle within the next five days. It was predicted that there would only be four days of trading left in February after the Lunar New Year. If most people wanted to postpone the settlement or swap until the deadline, the turmoil would be great. The market price yesterday went through circulation and stagnation, and there was nothing to describe. The overall trend was weak. From morning to night, each session had different and abnormal states of ups and downs, and the fluctuations were only around 5 fen and 1 jiao. The morale of the market was lax, and there were few transactions. It seemed that various firms were contracting. The result of the market price was that it was slightly more than 5 fen and 1 jiao and as high as 3 jiao and a half, while the 18th Customs Compilation and Dismissal and the 19th Customs Compilation were slightly better by 5 fen to 1-2 jiao. The cotton market was judged based on foreign cotton, and it was difficult to look down on.

Japanese Factories Gradually Increase Yarn Stockpiles

According to Shanghai Japanese cotton industry news, although the Fujian issue has come to an end, the approaching lunar new year and the financial pressure have made the actual demand in various places still sluggish. The market price has a gradual downward trend. On the one hand, after the Japanese Textile Federation withdrew its decision not to buy Indian cotton, it was predicted that the market price would tend to rise. US cotton also has the hope of establishing a production reduction, and it has risen to the 50 yuan level. As the situation resolves, Chinese cotton may follow foreign cotton and rise together. Therefore, Japanese factories in Shanghai are currently operating at full capacity, which will be disadvantageous. It was found that the yarn inventory at the end of last month was 15,685 bales, and it is feared that the yarn inventory statistics at the end of this month will exceed 20,000 bales. In the event of a deterioration of the situation, the warehouses will not have the capacity to accommodate them. Then, in April, some Japanese yarn factories may have to reduce their work.

The Flour Bidding Market Had Larger Buying Forces

Yesterday, the flour market was characterized by step-by-step construction in both the upper and lower markets. Because there were not many days left in the year, most factories stopped selling short. That is, even the current flour was unwilling to sell at a low price. The market has been rejected. However, scattered households in Beiyang and Tianjin needed to organize for the end of the year, and they would also absorb the far-month standard. Therefore, short covering and new hoarding and purchases were triggered. The market continued to step up. Also, factories did not dump, and many short sellers also stopped. All the few customer shorts and longs returned, so there were fewer transactions. The market stepped up. However, there are currently sufficient raw materials. The big gangs have not moved. The official surge in the market will have to wait until the red market. The closing price yesterday was 75 for February and May, 1 and a half for March, 1 for April, not open for June, and 1.75 for July.

Overseas Silk Sales Are Gradually Launched for Silk and Tea

New York Silk Prices Have All Been Rising Step by Step

Our port's American silk merchant firm received a telegram from New York yesterday, saying that most silk weaving factories have resumed work, the use of raw silk has gradually increased, and silk prices have all been rising step by step. The standard Japanese silk price converted to Chinese currency has broken through the 500 yuan mark. The price of grade B white factory silk with a uniformity of 81 fen and a count of 20-22 strips has also opened at 560-70 yuan.

The Source of Sichuan and Hubei Yellow Silk Has Been Stopped

Our port's Sichuan and Hubei yellow silk shops have all received express mail from silk shops in the place of origin, saying that the Yangtze River water is shallow, and river ships cannot directly transport. The shipment of Sichuan and Hubei yellow silk has been temporarily postponed, and normal shipment can only be made after the river transport is restored.

Sales of Yellow and White Factory Silk Have Gradually Moved

Each European and American estate in our port, in view of the rising prices of silk in New York and Lyon and the gradual rise in factory sales, has sent telegrams to Chinese silk merchants to discuss the matter. Telegrams for current yellow and white factory silk have been sent out a lot. Yesterday, Jardine Matheson and others entered 50 packages of yellow and white factory silk, and the price was still firm.

The Sales of Piece Goods Overcoat Woolen Cloth Have Come to an End

The sales of woolen cloth overcoats are now coming to an end. Because of the relationship between transportation and time, no one needs to charter it even if it is cheap. The streets are also unwilling to import more because the days for actual sales are gradually shortening. If there are orders, they will rather pay a high price to buy and cut them piecemeal. Therefore, those who have existing stocks of woolen overcoats are willing to sell them cheaply. Yesterday, a good Chinese colorful woolen overcoat was wholesaled for 5 yuan, but few people accepted it. There was still some retail business. Clothing shops priced each such overcoat at 30 foreign yuan, which was 3-4 yuan lower than last month. It is said that ordinary colorful woolen overcoats are now sold for more than 20 foreign yuan per piece.

Medical Field 216

Relocation of a Renowned Trauma Clinic: He Boyun, a famous trauma doctor and former medical consultant to the Guangdong Provincial Public Security Bureau Police Sports Association, is highly regarded for his expertise in treating injuries from falls, blows, knife wounds, and artillery fire, as well as for his skill in reconnecting fractured tendons and bones. His clinic, formerly located next to Hong An on Bazilu (Targets Road), has seen such a surge in patients that the original space became insufficient. He has now relocated to No. 44, Dekang Lane, Gesheng Road, Zhabei, where he will continue to provide consultations as usual. Furthermore, he is making his family's secret recipe for "Die Da Huan Hun Wan" (Trauma Revival Pills) available to the public at a particularly low price, aiming for widespread accessibility. Special discounts are offered for bulk purchases by large factories and organizations. It is also rumored that the Hangzhou Zhenqi-Shanghai Native Place Association has recently hired him as a long-term medical advisor.

From sterilization to tube filling, the entire process is completely mechanized and does not involve manual labor. The Bess-Tou intermittent three-stage sterilization method is used, resulting in a highly effective tonic. Each box contains twelve ampoules and is priced at $1.75. Letter to the Editor 222

Dear Editor, The accurate details of the Kailuan Coal Mine strike have been communicated in our previous letters, which we hope you have taken note of. We have now received a telegram from the Tianjin General Office on the 31st of last month, stating that the miners' strike was resolved on the 31st and that all mines have resumed work. Starting from the 1st of this month, all aspects of mining and transportation have returned to normal, etc. The Hakka people in various provinces along the Yangtze River, who usually use our coal, are quite concerned about this miners' strike. In order to clarify the truth for the Hakka people, we respectfully request that your newspaper disclose this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section. We would be very grateful. Respectfully, Kailuan Sales Office, Shanghai, February 2nd.

Reading Q&A

Reading and Low-Level Tastes (1) 223

|| Reply to Mr. He Chang (Continued)

We are very pleased that you are concerned about our "Reading Q&A." Although "Reading Q&A" has only been around for a month, the letters we have received from various places have all unanimously encouraged us, leaving us with no choice but to work harder. As for the standards you mentioned, they were originally what we had planned. The current discussions are all about general issues, which some readers may find too profound and empty, while others may find them too superficial and bordering on platitudes. These opinions all have some basis. When the other work of this section has not yet been done perfectly (for example, the Self-Study Series cannot be published immediately), those friends who are eager to get some concrete guidance will naturally feel unsatisfied, and for the general discussion, they will inevitably consider it profound. On the other hand, friends who already have considerable academic ability, after reading our discussions, scattered and unsystematic, which do not contain any profound or mysterious comments, will naturally consider them "platitudes" that are not worth considering. However, we also have our reasons. First, our original standard was to improve interest, which was set up for readers with general academic abilities that are not abundant. It is "not a garden specifically for intellectuals to explore academically," and we are extremely willing to make it ordinary, popular, and without any "mysterious and profound" elements. Second, we cannot cater to low-level tastes and must fight against them. In the future, we should gradually move from general discussions to smaller and more specific first questions, but the explanations should still strive for popularity, so that everyone who has not attended school can understand them. We believe that only when readers raise more concrete and practical questions will our guides be able to lead us to more practical solutions. We will definitely not disregard reality and artificially raise the standard of "guidance," unless it meets the general practical requirements of the readers.

Now, let's go further and briefly talk about how to overcome low-level tastes.

Undoubtedly, the majority of Shanghai citizens are still mired in low-level tastes. This expression can be seen not only in reading materials but also in entertainment and various life activities. This is true in everything. Generally speaking, this is a reflection of a kind of social and economic foundation, which is not surprising. We don’t need to have feelings of disgust or contempt for it, but we must fight against it to improve it because it also has a counter-effect on political and economic development. We cannot allow it to continue to spread. Now we are only talking about "low-level taste" reading materials, which are also the crystallization of feudal ideas, and it has the effect of binding the mind "upward" and "free." We cannot allow it to continue to exist and make everyone's life go backward.

Overcoming this taste is naturally not a simple matter and cannot be removed by an order. It is not just by your "enlightenment" that you will gain his conviction. The fundamental destructive power lies in the improvement of the general living environment of society, the improvement of education and cultural standards, and the gradual acquisition of a dominant position by new consciousness. Without being infatuated with the foundation of old bones, naturally, this kind of taste in reading materials cannot be produced. The Mandarin Ducks and Butterfly school still has a resurgence of power in China today, which is not without reason!

However, it is naturally our collective duty and practical need to accelerate their decline. However, the scope involved in this project includes criticism; the introduction of new works and the correction of all concepts, but as a whole, this section can naturally only do a small part of it. Moreover, what can be done now is to prevent everyone from eating morphine as a meal and replace it with a hygienic and nourishing food.

As for how to promote the gospel of "hygiene"? This is indeed a difficult task. For example, if his hobby is to read "Yu Li Hun" (Jade Pear Spirit), you must not immediately ask him to read Coal King, because these two "hobbies" are too far apart. Don't be afraid of trouble. You should introduce him to a book that is slightly more advanced than "Yu Li Hun" and the natures are not too far apart, such as "A Bundle of Love Letters" and give it to him to read. When he feels that the novels written in vernacular Chinese are interesting enough, you can take another step and send him a copy of Miyan (Lost Lamb) and gradually give him more high-level reading materials. When he has some awareness, you can introduce him to some more advanced or even very hard things, and he will no longer avoid it. This is how to lead the way.

In addition to this, of course, we should expand the ruthless criticism of low-level things ｜old｜, and expose its weaknesses in a popular and detailed way. On the active side, not only should there be new alternatives, but they should also be made "high" but not "deep." Regarding this point, we have a strong desire to compile some profound and famous things in a popular way, but this also depends on the efforts of everyone in society, not relying on a few individuals to succeed.

This section has decided to adopt the above methods for the "Reading Guidance" work. For the same two letters asking "How to start with literature," our answers may be completely different. If a person has some foundation, we will directly introduce him to some high-level hobbies. If someone likes "antiques" very much, then we will not rush to make him do an impossible long jump, but only introduce some appetite-stimulating agents to change his taste. Therefore, this kind of work is more troublesome than school education, but it is very practical. Therefore, this part of the work can only be answered and cannot be published in the "Reading Q&A" column. In terms of form, there may be some contradictions in our draft replies, but this is a certain order in the unified education process.

Finally, we hope that Mr. He and the enthusiastic teachers will give serious criticism to the above remarks.

Chunqiu

Solution 224

— Hua Ling

A solution, regardless of the time, place, matter, or environment, is an indispensable treasure.

If you unintentionally win the lottery but did not pre-plan a life outline after winning before the draw, you will naturally frown and roll your eyes, trying to figure out a way to handle this huge amount of money. Otherwise, you will be at a loss.

Looking out the window, you happen to see the bedroom of a modern woman. If you want to have a secret tryst with this modern woman, you must come up with a solution. If this modern woman is interested in you, but you are a stubborn man and insist on remaining indifferent, then you need to think of a way to avoid trouble.

A big guy is fighting with a little kid. The big guy's head is cracked open, and the little kid's arm is broken. The patrolman dozing under the eaves strides over, hails two rickshaws, and sends them to the hospital. This is also one of the solutions.

If a husband gambles, drinks, and engages in prostitution, neglecting the family and ignoring household expenses, or if one encounters a fierce, unreasonable wife, the opposing party will always have to think carefully and come up with a solution.

"When water comes, use earth to block it; when soldiers come, use generals to resist" is an example. At the same time, the empty city ploy, offering a map, and the surrender of the naked king are undeniable solutions. Burning books and burying scholars is, of course, an excellent way to prevent rebellion.

Therefore, we don't need to curse civil war because civil war is a way for some people to find a way out. We don't need to curse "don't become an official if there's no one in court" because this is a way for those in court to help their poor relatives and friends.

After a mess, we always see the adults stroking their beards and saying, "We must come up with a way to deal with the aftermath." Although whether this method can be implemented and whether it can be effectively handled are unknown, "we must think of a way" is always a self-evident truth.

When there's no solution, commit suicide. In fact, "suicide" is a solution. Therefore, I believe that only those who live under the slogan of "no solution" are the most helpless people in the world and should suffer.

Year-End in the Countryside 225

— Chi Fo

"On a plate from the distant market, no delicacies are found,

In a jar from the poor home, only old wine is drawn;

I can talk with the old neighbor face to face,

Across the fence, I call him to drink the remaining cup."

This poem by Du Gongbu (Du Fu) describes the joyful interactions between friends and neighbors in the countryside, which seems more genuine than opening champagne and eating fancy meals in the city. In winter, the countryside is filled with piles of rice, wheat, taro, and yams; many vegetables are planted in the fields; many chickens, ducks, pigs, and sheep are raised in the pens; the old wife weaves many bolts of homespun cloth; the daughter cooks fragrant rice; and the son brews strong wine. There's no need to buy coal with money, and there's no need to install water heaters, prepare electric furnaces, or burn animal charcoal and firewood to keep warm and cook meals. None of the essential elements of life—clothing, food, and shelter—require relying on others; they are readily available. Can city dwellers enjoy this kind of simple pleasure?

Although living in humble thatched huts, they still breathe fresh air, bask in warm sunlight, look at distant mountains, and listen to flowing water. The smoke, clouds, flying birds, green trees, and blue clouds are there for them to enjoy every day. In the city, what allows you to enjoy this? Rushing around anxiously, faces covered in dust, what's the point? What's the point?

The grim shadows of the city envelop people, and cunning, deceit, ferocity, madness... and sickness are all revealed. As the cold weather arrives and the year draws to a close, the city reveals an increasingly distressed face. In the countryside, with fragrant wine and rice, basking in the sun and chatting idly, talking only about mulberry and hemp and not asking about governance and disorder, they are truly the "favored ones of heaven." Although it is said that the countryside is bankrupt, after all, places without bandits are better than the city.

Night's Weariness 226

— Hu Defang

Some people say that night is ugly because people hide under the curtain of darkness and do all kinds of irrational things; once it's night, the kind becomes evil, and the pure becomes filthy. But is this because of the night's mysterious seduction that makes it so? Or do the people wearing false masks reveal their true colors? Some people also say that night is beautiful, that night is so quiet, the moonlight is so gentle, the stars blinking with their delicate eyes are so lovely, the towering height of the pagoda, the tinkling of flowing water by the stream, the swaying of flower branches and tree shadows, and the dong-dong of cold rain knocking on the window, what the Lord shows in the night is a hundred times more full of poetry, allowing people to chant or sing praises; night has infinitely beautiful posture, at least in the eyes of an enthusiast.

Like me, I can't curse it because of the ugliness of the night, and I won't praise it just because it has such beauty. Night only gives me a kind of goodwill, and this goodwill makes me remember it when I am working because it allows me to enthusiastically hook me into its arms after a day's work of weariness. I rest, unusually sweet, quiet, all evil thoughts, all illusory pursuits, go far away, go far away, I sometimes even hear laughter in my dreams, night makes me dependent, although we still have to part at that time.

The sky is becoming more and more hazy, and the space is like countless layers of green-gray smoke floating. The teacher bird shot past like an arrow, and in the blur, it seemed to disappear into the clouds. Ah Hua can only open half an eye to look at you, although she is still leaning at your feet; under the sweet sleep of the little sister, picture postcards, harmonicas, and song collections are also scattered and snuggling together; the chicks can't find their mother and close their eyes, constantly chirping and looking up... This is a picture of "Night Weariness," and night also covers the world with a thin veil at this time.

Bamboo Wife and Tang Pozi (Hot Water Bottle) 227

— Yi Yi Guan Zhu

In the scorching summer that makes people dizzy, after a day of hard work, you want to rest at night, but the heat is so oppressive that even if you don't wear a thread and wave a large palm fan, you will still sweat and find it difficult to fall asleep. At this time, if you have a bamboo wife to hug you to sleep, you will feel cool all over and comfortable throughout your body. Naturally, your soul will leave your body and you will no longer suffer from the heat. Because the bamboo wife is not only naturally beautiful but also has icy skin and snowy flesh. Just imagine having such a beautiful bamboo wife to hug you to sleep, a great blessing, what else do you want? If you still complain about the heat, then only "Heaven knows"! Therefore, the bamboo wife is a beloved object in the summer, especially for burly guys, who cannot do without her. But when the golden wind brings coolness and the oppressive heat disappears completely, sleeping at night already feels as cool as water. Then, the bamboo wife at this time, is just like youth that has passed, no longer suitable, and will be abandoned like an autumn fan!

As for the Tang Pozi (hot water bottle), as soon as we hear her name, we know that she is a wizened old woman with wrinkled skin and white hair, fat and short, and of a fiery temperament. Where does she have the naturally beautiful icy skin and snowy flesh like the bamboo wife? She also does not have the gentle and considerate elegant attitude of the bamboo wife! It is always thought that no one likes her. However, that's not the case. Who knows that in this cold and freezing winter season, it is precisely the time when the Tang Pozi is triumphant. If you don't believe me, look at the general people in this cold night, who doesn't want to pull the Tang Pozi into the quilt to share a warm dream? No matter how ugly the Tang Pozi is, everyone only knows to passionately love her, and will not get tired of her. Do you think it's strange?

Although, I feel from this that the ups and downs of life are also like this. For example, when people get you, they can't wait to hold you up to the thirty-third heaven. When they don't need you, they can't wait to throw you down to the eighteenth level of hell, and even kicking you would be good. Alas! Looking at it this way, the warmth and coldness of human relationships are originally uncertain. Then, what's so strange about the bamboo wife and the Tang Pozi being liked and disliked at times?

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 228

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Three

Unable to bear the pain, he listened intently to the music.

The happy time was not enough; he hastened to leave upon the arrival of a telegram.

After hearing these words from Jiang, she stood there dumbfounded, looking at him and saying, "Could it be that the situation outside the pass isn't very good?" Zi Qiang smiled and said, "It's not that bad, not that it's that bad." As he was saying this, Gui Zhi, who was sitting in the new room, heard it. Holding the door curtain, leaning diagonally against the door frame, she looked at Zhao Ziqiang and asked, "Just now, a guest came from the city to deliver a telegram to you, right?" Zhao Ziqiang nodded and replied yes. Gui Zhi looked at her mother, then looked at her husband, deliberately calming herself down, and asked in a very gentle voice, "Can I see your telegram?" How could Zhao Ziqiang disobey his new wife? He had to slowly pull the telegram out of his pocket and hand it to Gui Zhi with both hands. When she received it and looked at it, it read:

To Zhao Ziqiang, Company Commander, Hengfeng Rice Store, Xizhimen Avenue, Beiping, as per the instructions of the regimental commander, you are ordered to return to the defense immediately. Do not delay. Must not delay. Battalion Commander Bao Fang.

By chance, Gui Zhi completely recognized the words on the telegram. Holding the telegram paper with both hands, she trembled uncertainly, and the words in her heart were self-evident.

Chapter Twenty-Four

Pouring wine and serving meals, wild celebration with farewell tears

Lighting a lamp to warm dreams, chanting softly through the long night

Everyone knew that Zhao Ziqiang's return home to get married this time was a short stay, but he was leaving in less than a week. This was something that Zhao Ziqiang himself had not expected. Zhao Weng heard about the telegram from inside the house, stuck his head out to look, and then saw the three people standing in the hall, in that state, and he understood in his heart. So, he corrected his expression and said to Ziqiang, "The body of a soldier belongs to the country. It is already very rare for you to be able to ask for leave to come back and get married. Since Battalion Commander Bao has sent a telegram, you should quickly return to the camp." If the situation is a little peaceful, I also want to go to see the outside of the pass. I will take Gui Zhi and Old Mrs. Yang to Xifengkou." (237)
